            Section TieLine_Input_Data {
                DeclarationSection InterchangeTransaction {
                    Set ItsSet {
                        Text: "FLOWGATE OF INTERCHANGE TRASACTION";
                        Index: its;
                    }
                    StringParameter ItsEName {
                        IndexDomain: (its);
                    }
                    StringParameter ItsCName {
                        IndexDomain: (its);
                    }
                    Parameter ItsTielineList {
                        IndexDomain: (its,tie);
                        Range: binary;
                    }
                    Parameter ItsPowerPlan {
                        IndexDomain: (its,t);
                    }
                    Parameter ItsPowerPrice {
                        IndexDomain: (its,t);
                    }
                }
                DeclarationSection TieLinePara {
                    Parameter tiePmax {
                        IndexDomain: (tie);
                    }
                    Parameter tiePmin {
                        IndexDomain: (tie);
                    }
                    StringParameter tieFrom {
                        IndexDomain: (tie);
                    }
                    StringParameter tieTo {
                        IndexDomain: (tie);
                    }
                    Parameter tiePrice {
                        IndexDomain: (tie,t);
                    }
                    Parameter TMP_tiecost {
                        Definition: sum[(tie,t) , tieCost(tie,t)];
                    }
                }
                DeclarationSection TieLinePlan {
                    Set TieLineFixedPowerSet {
                        SubsetOf: (TieLineSet,Periods);
                    }
                    Parameter TieLineFixedP {
                        IndexDomain: (tie,t) in TieLineFixedPowerSet;
                    }
                }
                DeclarationSection TieLineRunDecomPara {
                    Parameter TieDecomRate {
                        IndexDomain: (tie,t);
                        Default: 1;
                    }
                    Parameter TieIsRun {
                        IndexDomain: (tie,t);
                        Default: 0;
                    }
                }
            }

                Procedure CCUModeInitStatusSet {
                    Body: {
                        for(ccu) do
                        
                        
                        
                                mInitStatus(ccu , InitMode(ccu) ) := 1 ;
                        
                                mInitPower(ccu , InitMode(ccu) ) := InitP(ccu) ;
                        
                                !! Correct the Current Mode
                                mInitOffTime(ccu , InitMode(ccu) ) := 0 ;
                                mInitOnTime(ccu , InitMode(ccu) ) := InitTime(ccu);
                        
                        
                                if( InitMode(ccu) = first(ModeSet) ) then
                                        mInitPower(ccu,m) := 0;
                                endif;
                        
                        endfor;
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        Uc(ccu,m,'past') :=  mInitStatus(ccu,m);
                        mP(ccu,m,'past') :=  mInitPower(ccu,m);
                        ccu_ui(ccu,gt,'past') := sum[m, mInitStatus(ccu,m)*ModeGTList(ccu,m,gt)];
                    }
                }
            }

                            max( 0 , FixedOnOffList(ele,t) - FixedOnOffList(ele,t-1) );
                        }
                        Comment: "xuebike added 20150414";

                    Parameter zi_p {
                        IndexDomain: (ele ,t) in FixedOnOffSet;
                        Range: binary;

                Procedure FormModeFixedOnOff {
                    Body: {
                        !! CCU 0ne-unit mainteance to mode maintance
                        /*for(ele , t) in FixedOnOffSet | FixedOnOffList(ele,t) = 0 do
                        
                                if(ele in GTSet) then
                        
                                        for(ccu,m) | ModeGTList(ccu,m,ele)=1 do
                                                ModeFixedOnOffSet := ModeFixedOnOffSet + {(ccu,m,t)} ;
                                                ModeFixedOnOffList(ccu,m,t) := 0 ;
                                        endfor;
                        
                                endif;
                        
                        
                                if(ele in STSet) then
                        
                                        for(ccu,m) | ModeSTList(ccu,m,ele)=1 do
                                                ModeFixedOnOffSet := ModeFixedOnOffSet + {(ccu,m,t)} ;
                                                ModeFixedOnOffList(ccu,m,t) := 0 ;
                                        endfor;
                        
                                endif;
                        
                        
                        endfor;
                        */
                        
                        !! CCU 0ne-unit must-run/off to mode must-run/off   MODIFY BY G.J. 2009-12-24
                        
                        for(ele , t) in FixedOnOffSet | FixedOnOffList(ele,t)=0 do
                        
                                if(ele in GTSet) then
                        
                                        for(ccu,m) | ModeGTList(ccu,m,ele)=1 do
                                                ModeFixedOnOffSet := ModeFixedOnOffSet + {(ccu,m,t)} ;
                                                ModeFixedOnOffList(ccu,m,t) := FixedOnOffList(ele,t) ;
                                        endfor;
                        
                                endif;
                        
                        
                                if(ele in STSet) then
                        
                                        for(ccu,m) | ModeSTList(ccu,m,ele)=1 do
                                                ModeFixedOnOffSet := ModeFixedOnOffSet + {(ccu,m,t)} ;
                                                ModeFixedOnOffList(ccu,m,t) := FixedOnOffList(ele,t) ;
                                        endfor;
                        
                                endif;
                        
                        
                        endfor;
                    }
                }

        Section Solution {
            Procedure MainExecution {
                Body: {
                    EmptyAllIdentifiers;!xuebike edit 20150414.
                    
                        Data_Init_by_Hands;
                    
                    
                    
                    ! ReadXlsData;
                    
                    ORG_Load(t):=sum[nd,BusLoad(nd,t)];
                     CopyFirstPrdPTDFAndLossData;
                    
                     Data_Check;
                    if(IsOpt=1) then
                       FormConstSet;
                       SCUCInit;
                    
                       if EdMode=0 then !scuc lmp calculation:first calculate uc then calculate ed.!xuebike edited 20160720 pi
                          solve UCFeeLeast;
                    
                          !!write out the uc result.
                          e_scuc_result_out;
                    
                          !!refresh the unit onoff status according to the uc result.
                          !empty LMPSolutionConsSet;
                          FormConstSet;
                          SCUCInit_Again;
                          solve FeeLeast;
                          e_file_out;
                       elseif EdMode=1 then !sced lmp calculate: calculate ed directly.!xuebike edited 20160720
                          solve FeeLeast;
                          e_file_out;
                       endif;
                    endif;
                }
            }
            Procedure SCUCInit {
                Body: {
                        for (i,t)|(i,t) in FixedOnOffSet do
                    
                            Ui(i,t).nonvar := 1;
                    	Ui(i,t) := FixedOnOffList(i,t);
                    
                    	if(t>'past') then
                    		yi(i,t) := max( 0 , Ui(i,t) - Ui(i,t-1) );
                            	zi(i,t) := max( 0 , Ui(i,t-1) - Ui(i,t) );
                            endif;
                        endfor;
                }
                Comment: {
                    "!xuebike edit 20150414"
                }
            }
            Procedure SCUCInit_Again {
                Body: {
                        for (i,t) do
                    
                            Ui(i,t).nonvar := 1;
                    
                    	if(t>'past') then
                    		yi(i,t) := max( 0 , Ui(i,t) - Ui(i,t-1) );
                            	zi(i,t) := max( 0 , Ui(i,t-1) - Ui(i,t) );
                            endif;
                        endfor;
                }
            }
            Procedure EmptyAllIdentifiers {
                Body: {
                    !empty AllIdentifiers;
                    empty  LMPSolutionConsSet;
                }
                Comment: {
                    "!xuebike edit 20150414"
                }
            }
            Procedure Data_Init_by_Hands {
                Body: {
                    !Path_in := ".\\16384101_312000165_scuc";
                    
                    !Path_in := ".\\16384101_312000165_scuc_control_is_zero";
                    
                    !!Path_in := ".\\16384103_20120926_succ";
                    
                    !GFG_path_in := ".\\16384102_312000448_scuc\\2";
                    Path_in :=".\\Input";
                    
                    Path_out := ".\\Output";
                    Data_check_path :=".\\Output";
                    
                    
                    Data_Init;
                }
            }
            Procedure FormSCUCConstraints {
                Body: {
                    empty SCUCConstraintsSet;
                    !C.H.H 2012-10-10
                    if IsNFG then
                            SCUCConstraintsSet +=
                                    data{
                                            NormalFlowGateConstraints
                                            !,NFGCons !xuebike edit 20150422
                                            !GeneratedFlowGateConstraints ,
                                            !GFGCons
                                           } ;
                    endif;
                    
                    
                    
                    if IsMaxGroupInjection then
                            SCUCConstraintsSet +=
                                    data{
                                             !! RegionVoltagePowerConstraints,
                                            ItsNetPmaxPowerConstraint,
                                            RegionVoltagePowerConstraints_Down
                                         } ;
                    endif;
                    
                    SCUCConstraintsSet +=
                    data
                       {
                    
                       !! totalcost
                       TieLineFixedPowerCons       ,!!xuebike 2014.09.02 for tieline optimiazation
                    
                       !FixedUi                      ,   !!MODIFY BY GJ 2009-12-17
                       FixedPower                  ,!!xuebike 2014.09.02 for tieline optimiazation
                    
                       OutagePmaxPowerConstraints, OutagePminPowerConstraints,!!xuebike 2014.09.02 for tieline optimiazation
                    
                      /* C.H.H 2012-10-10
                         ModeFixedOnOffConstraints  ,
                        ModeFixedPowerConstraints ,
                      */
                        fixedOnOffConstraints,!!xuebike 2014.09.02 for tieline optimiazation
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                        !! UnitReserveConstraints       ,
                    
                        !! Energy Group
                        HydroEnergyConstraints_Up       ,    HydroEnergyConstraints_Down  !!xuebike 2014.09.02 for tieline optimiazation
                    /*
                        !! Power Group
                        RegionVoltagePowerConstraints,    RegionVoltagePowerConstraints_Down      ,
                    
                        !! reserve Group
                        RegionReservePowerConstraints,     RegionReservePowerConstraints_Down
                    
                    */
                    
                    
                     }
                    
                    
                    + SystemConstraintsSet
                    + UCConstraintsSet
                    ! C.H.H  2012-10-10  CCUConstraintsSet
                    +TieLineConstraintsSet
                    ! + ItsConstraintsSet;
                    
                    +ZJCommonConsSet
                    +PowerBiasConsSet;
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    if IsMultiStartUp then
                            SCUCConstraintsSet +=
                            data{
                                    !!********   CCU Unit multistartup cost ***********   Z.Y.T.  & G.J. 2010-4-20
                                   InitCCUCold1Trans4CostConstraint,
                                    InitCCUWarmA1Trans4CostConstraint,
                                    InitCCUWarmB1Trans4CostConstraint,
                                    CCUCold1Trans4CostConstraint,
                                    CCUWarmA1Trans4CostConstraint,
                                    CCUWarmB1Trans4CostConstraint,
                                    InitCCUCold2Trans5CostConstraint,
                                    InitCCUWarmA2Trans5CostConstraint,
                                    InitCCUWarmB2Trans5CostConstraint,
                                    CCUCold2Trans5CostConstraint,
                                    CCUWarmA2Trans5CostConstraint,
                                    CCUWarmB2Trans5CostConstraint,
                                    InitCCUCold4Trans6CostConstraint,
                                    InitCCUWarmA4Trans6CostConstraint,
                                    InitCCUWarmB4Trans6CostConstraint,
                                    CCUCold4Trans6CostConstraint,
                                    CCUWarmA4Trans6CostConstraint,
                                    CCUWarmB4Trans6CostConstraint,
                                    InitCCUCold5Trans6CostConstraint,
                                    InitCCUWarmA5Trans6CostConstraint,
                                    InitCCUWarmB5Trans6CostConstraint,
                                    CCUCold5Trans6CostConstraint,
                                    CCUWarmA5Trans6CostConstraint,
                                    CCUWarmB5Trans6CostConstraint,
                                    CCUCold3Trans6CostConstraint
                            };
                    
                    
                    endif;
                }
            }
            Procedure Data_Init {
                Body: {
                    control_inf_input_ext(path_in);

                    UnitTimeStartPrice_Init;

                     if  (ClearingMode=0)then!PriceClearing
                      CostBlockStart(i,l,t):=PriceBlockStart(i,l,t);
                      CostBlockEnd(i,l,t):=PriceBlockEnd(i,l,t);
                      UnitBaseCost(i,l,t):=UnitBasePrice(i,l,t);
                      UnitIncCost(i,l,t):=UnitIncPrice(i,l,t);
                      Time_ColdStartCost(i,t):=Time_ColdStartPrice(i,t);
                    elseif(ClearingMode=1)then !CostClearing
                      CostBlockStart(i,l,t):=CostBlockStart(i,l,t);
                      CostBlockEnd(i,l,t):=CostBlockEnd(i,l,t);
                      UnitBaseCost(i,l,t):=UnitBaseCost(i,l,t);
                      UnitIncCost(i,l,t):=UnitIncCost(i,l,t);
                      Time_ColdStartCost(i,t):=Time_ColdStartCost(i,t);
                    endif;
                    !!###############
                    
                    
                    !ThermalOS_UnitPowerLimitTemp_Init ;
                    
                    !!InitialState_Init ;
                    Thermal_ele_initialState_Init ;
                    
                    InitializeNeededVariables ;
                    
                    ! C.H.H. 2012-10-10 UnitReducePower_Init; !!for CCA reduce power.
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    !! ******************* Input the CCUnit data *******************
                     /*  C.H.H. 2012-10-10

                    CCUnitModeFixOnOffInit; !!for ccu mode fix on off. Added by Zh.Y.T. 2010-3-24
                    CCUModeOffTimeInit; !!Added By Zh.Y.T. 2010-3-30

                    CCUGasHeatRateInit; !!Added By Zh.Y.T. 2011-1-20
                    CCUnitHeat_Init;  !!Added By Zh.Y.T. 2011-1-20
                    
                    **/

                    !TieLine_Init ;
                    !TieLineCost_Init ;
                    !TieLineFixPower_Init ; !!xuebike 2013.01.21 for tieline optimiazation
                    /*
                    TieLineRunDecomPara_Init;  !! ADDED BY G.J. 2009-11-24

                    /*  C.H.H. 2012-10-10

                    ItsEnergy_Input_Init ;
                    
                    
                    
                    !!******************** Input the Power Group data ****************
                    RegionVoltage_Init ;
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    !!******************** Input the Reserve Group data ****************
                    !! RegionReserve_Init ;
                    
                    
                    
                    !!******************** Input the Resourcr Group data ****************
                    ResourceGroup_Init ;
                    
                    
                    !!******************** Input the Environment Group data ****************
                    EnvironmentGroup_Init
                    
                    */
                    
                    Pmax(i,t) := Reg_Pmax(i);
                    Pmin(i,t) := Reg_Pmin(i);
                    /*  C.H.H. 2012-10-10
                    mPmax(ccu,m,t) := Reg_mPmax(ccu,m) ;
                    mPmin(ccu,m,t) := Reg_mPmin(ccu,m) ;
                    
                    
                    if IsCaseSequence = 0 then
                    
                         Data_Assign_Through_Control_Para ;
                    
                    endif;
                    
                    
                    FormModeFixedOnOff ;  !! Form CCU fiexed on/off  G.J. 2010-1-21
                    
                    if IsRunningCost = 0 then
                            for (ccu,gst) do
                                    CCURunningCost(ccu,gst) := 0;
                            endfor;
                    endif;
                    if IsEsCost = 0 then
                            for (ccu,m,m2) do
                                    ColdTransCost(ccu,m,m2) := 0;
                                    WarmATransCost(ccu,m,m2) := 0;
                                    WarmBTransCost(ccu,m,m2) := 0;
                                    HotTransCost(ccu,m,m2) := 0;
                            endfor;
                    endif;
                    
                    */
                    
                    
                    !TieDirection_Init;
                    
                    
                    !CalTotalCap;!xuebike edit 20150620
                    
                     !! Move it from Data_Assign_Through_Control_Para to here G.J. 2010-1-23
                    
                    !!lmp,pi
                    pNode_Init;
                    Line_Init;
                    BusLoad_Init;
                    PtdfSens_Init;
                    SysLossPenaltyFactor_Init;
                    SysTotalLoss_Init;
                    NdUnitList_Init;
                }
            }
            Procedure Data_Check {
                Body: {
                    IsOpt :=1;
                    
                    put Erro_Information_file;
                    Erro_Information_file.pagewidth := 5000;
                    put "********************* !!! Erro Information !!!!!!!!!!!!!!!***********************",/;
                    
                    ! ******************* Check the Load data **********************
                    
                    for t do
                            block
                                    if Load(t) <= 0 then
                                            IsOpt :=0;
                                            put "Fatal!!!"," ",Load_Time(t)," ","Load = ",load(t),",MainExcution over",/;
                                            !break;
                                    endif;
                                    if sum[i| FixedOnOffList(i,t) <> 0 and not (i,t)  in FixedScheduleSet,Pmax(i,t)] + sum[i| FixedOnOffList(i,t) <> 0 and (i,t) in FixedScheduleSet,Pi(i,t)]  < load(t) then
                                    endif;
                    
                            endblock;
                    endfor;
                    
                    ! ******************* Check the Pmin & Pmax data **********************
                    for (i,t) do
                            block
                                    if (Pmin(i,t) > Pmax(i,t)) then
                                            IsOpt :=0;
                                            put "# Fatal!!!"," ",cName(i)," ",Load_Time(t)," ,the maximum power is",Pmax(i,t),"and the minimum Power is",Pmin(i,t),"the maximum power is smallar than the minimum power,MainExcution over",/;
                                    endif;
                            endblock;
                    
                    
                    endfor;
                    !******************** check the Fixed on off  ***********************
                    for (i,t)   do
                            block
                            if  EnvironmentUnitOffList(i,t) <> ResourceUnitOnOffList(i,t)| (i,t) in ResourceUnitOnOffset and (i,t) in EnvironmentUnitOffSet   then
                                    IsOpt :=0;
                                    put "Fatal Erro!!! ",Load_Time(t),"The Resource Constraint required that the status of ",cName(i)," is ",ResourceUnitOnOffList(i,t),/;
                                    put "but the Enviroment constarint required that the status of ",cName(i)," is ",EnvironmentUnitOffList(i,t),/;
                            endif;
                    
                            if  UnPlanedMaintenaceList(i,t) <> ResourceUnitOnOffList(i,t)| (i,t) in UnPlanedMaintenanceSet and (i,t) in ResourceUnitOnOffset   then
                                    IsOpt :=0;
                                    put "Fatal Erro!!! ",Load_Time(t),"The Operation Constraint required that the status of ",cName(i)," is ",UnPlanedMaintenaceList(i,t),/;
                                    put "but the Resource constarint required that the status of ",cName(i)," is ",ResourceUnitOnOffList(i,t),/;
                            endif;
                    
                            if  UnPlanedMaintenaceList(i,t) <> EnvironmentUnitOffList(i,t)| (i,t) in UnPlanedMaintenanceSet and (i,t) in EnvironmentUnitOffSet   then
                                    IsOpt :=0;
                                    put "Fatal Erro!!! ",Load_Time(t),"The Operation Constraint required that the status of ",cName(i)," is ",UnPlanedMaintenaceList(i,t),/;
                                    put "but the Enviroment constarint required that the status of ",cName(i)," is ",EnvironmentUnitOffList(i,t),/;
                            endif;
                            endblock;
                    
                    endfor;
                    
                    !*************************************  check the fixed power ********************************************
                    for (i,t)|(i,t) in FixedScheduleSet and not ((i,t) in IsTestUnit) do
                    
                            if FixedOutPutPower(i,t) > 0 and FixedOutPutPower(i,t) < Pmin(i,t) then
                                    IsOpt := 0;
                                    put "Erro!!! The fixed power is smaller than the mimimum power!!!",/;
                                    put formatstring("%e",i)," ",load_time(t)," , The fixed power is",FixedOutPutPower(i,t),"and the minimum power is",Pmin(i,t),/;
                            endif;
                            if FixedOutPutPower(i,t) > Pmax(i,t) then
                                    IsOpt := 0;
                                    put "Erro!!! The fixed power is bigger than the maximum power!!!",/;
                                    put formatstring("%e",i)," ",load_time(t)," , The fixed power is",FixedOutPutPower(i,t),"and the maximum power is",Pmax(i,t),/;
                            endif;
                    
                            if(((i,t) in FixedScheduleSet) and ((i ,t) in FixedOnOffSet)) then
                                    if (FixedOutPutPower(i,t) > 0 and FixedOnOffList(i,t)=0) or  (FixedOutPutPower(i,t) = 0 and FixedOnOffList(i,t)=1) then
                                            IsOpt:=0;
                                            put formatstring("Error!! %e",i)," ",load_time(t)," , The fixed power conflict with the fix UI, FixPower is ",FixedOutPutPower(i,t),"and the fixUI is",FixedOnOffList(i,t),/;
                                    endif;
                            endif;
                    endfor;
                    
                    !************************ check the rampUp and rampDown constraints (sced)********************
                    for i do
                      if ((Pmin(i,'period-1') - InitPower(i)) >  RampUp(i)*PrdMin*InitStatus(i)) and InitStatus(i) = 1 then
                            IsOpt := 0;
                            put formatstring("%e",i)," ",cName(i)," Initial Power =",InitPower(i),",  Min power = ",Pmin(i,'period-1'),", RampUp Power =",RampUp(i)*PrdMin*InitStatus(i)," ",Load_Time('period-1'),
                                 " : Fatal!!!, The Initial power schedule don't satisfy the rampUp constraint, MainExection over!",/;
                      endif;
                      if InitPower(i) - Pmax(i,'Period-1') > RampDown(i)*PrdMin*InitStatus(i) and InitStatus(i) = 1  then
                            IsOpt := 0;
                            put formatstring("%e",i)," ",cName(i)," Initial Power =",InitPower(i)," , Max Power =",Pmax(i,'period-1')," , RampDown Power =", RampDown(i)*PrdMin*InitStatus(i)," ",Load_Time('period-1'),
                                                    " : Fatal!!!, The Initial power schedule don't satisfy the rampDown constraint, MainExection over!",/;
                      endif;
                    endfor;
                    ! *************************  check the initial status and the initiaol power _20101125_  infeasible RampUpconstraints case_time 20101126 *******
                    for i do
                            if InitPower(i) > 0 and InitStatus(i) = 0 then
                                    Isopt := 0;
                                    put Formatstring("%e",i)," ,the initial power is not in accord with the initial status";
                                    put " the initial power is ",InitPower(i)," and the initial status is ",InitStatus(i),", MainExecution over!!",/;
                            endif;
                            if InitPower(i) = 0 and InitStatus(i) = 1 then
                                    IsOpt:=0;
                                    put Formatstring("%e",i)," ,the initial power is not in in accord with the initial status";
                                    put "the initial power is",InitPower(i),"and the initial status is",InitStatus(i),", MainExecution over!!",/;
                            endif;
                    
                            if InitPower(i)> 1.1*Reg_Pmax(i) then
                                    IsOpt:=0;
                                    put Formatstring("Error, %e",i)," ,the initial power is bigger than the 1.1 multiply pmax";
                                    put " the initial power is ",InitPower(i),"and the 1.1 multiply pmax is ",1.1*Reg_Pmax(i),"!!",/;
                            endif ;
                            /*
                            if InitPower(i)< 0.6*Capacity(i) then
                                    put Formatstring("%e",i)," ,the initial power is too lesser ";
                                    put " the initial power is",InitPower(i),"and the check value is",0.6*Capacity(i),"!!",/;
                            endif ;
                            */
                            if InitPower(i)< Reg_Pmin(i) and InitStatus(i) = 1 then
                                    put Formatstring("Error, %e",i)," ,the initial power is less than the pmin";
                                    put " the initial power is",InitPower(i),"and the pmin is",Reg_Pmin(i),"!!",/;
                            endif ;
                    
                            !!********************xuebike edit 20150414
                            if(InitStatus(i)=0 and InitOffTime(i)<>NT) then
                                    IsOpt:=0;
                                    Put Formatstring("%e",i),", the InitOffTime is not equal NT";
                                    put " ,and the NT is:,",NT/;
                            endif;
                    
                            if(InitStatus(i)=1 and InitOnTime(i)<>NT) then
                                    IsOpt:=0;
                                    Put Formatstring("%e",i),", the InitOnTime is not equal NT";
                                    put " ,and the NT is:,",NT/;
                            endif;
                    
                            if(InitStatus(i)=0 and sum[t | t<=element( Periods,( 1+ DTi(i) ) ), FixedOnOffList(i,t)] <>0) then
                                    IsOpt:=0;
                                    Put FormatString("Fatal Error: %e",i)," ,The Given OnOff status violate the InitialOffConstraint!!!!!"/;
                            endif;
                    
                            if(InitStatus(i)=1 and sum[t | t<=element( Periods,(1+ UTi(i) ) and t>(element(Periods,0)) ), (1-FixedOnOffList(i,t))] <>0)then
                                    IsOpt:=0;
                                    Put FormatString("Fatal Error: %e",i)," ,The Given OnOff status violate the InitialRunConstriant!!!!!!"/;
                            endif;
                    
                    
                    endfor;
                    
                    for (i,t)| t>element( Periods,( 1+UTi(i) ) ) do!!xuebike added 20150414
                      if(yi_p(i,t) + sum[ j| j>=t+1 and j<= element(Periods, min(NT, Ord(t,periods)-1+MinOnTime(i)-1 )+1),zi_p(i,j)] >1) then
                        IsOpt:=0;
                        Put FormatString("Fatal Error: %e from %e ",i,t)," ,The Given OnOff status violate the UnitMinUpConstraint!!!!!!"/;
                      endif;
                    
                    endfor;
                    
                    for(i,t)|t>element( Periods,( 1+ DTi(i) )) do !!xuebike added 20150414
                      if(zi_p(i,t) + sum[ k| k>=t+1 and k<= element(Periods, min(NT, Ord(t,periods)-1+MinOffTime(i)-1 )+1 ),yi_p(i,k)] >1) then
                        IsOpt:=0;
                        Put FormatString("Fatal Error: %e from %e",i,t)," ,The Given OnOff status violate the UnitMinUpConstraint!!!!!!"/;
                      endif;
                    endfor;
                    
                    for hdp do !!xuebike added 20150520
                      tempFloat:=0;
                      tempFloat1:=0;
                    
                      if(HydroEnergyLimitDown(hdp)>HydroEnergyLimit(hdp)) then
                         IsOpt:=0;
                         put Formatstring("Fatal Error!! HydroPlant %e",hdp)," ,energy down limit is bigger than up limit, down limit is: ",HydroEnergyLimitDown(hdp)," and up limit is: ",HydroEnergyLimitDown(hdp),/;
                      endif;
                    
                      for i do
                        if HydroPlantUnitList(hdp,i)=1 then
                           for t| t >= 'period-1' do
                             if((i,t) in FixedOnOffSet) then
                                tempFloat:=tempFloat+FixedOnOffList(i,t)*Reg_Pmax(i)*PrdMin / 60;
                                tempFloat1:=tempFloat1+FixedOnOffList(i,t)*Reg_Pmin(i)*PrdMin / 60;
                             else
                                tempFloat:=tempFloat+Reg_Pmax(i)*PrdMin / 60;
                                !tempFloat1:=tempFloat1+Reg_Pmin(i)*PrdMin / 60;
                             endif;
                    
                           endfor;
                    
                        endif;
                      endfor;
                      if(tempFloat<HydroEnergyLimitDown(hdp)) then
                        IsOpt:=0;
                        put Formatstring("Fatal Error!! HydroPlant %e",hdp)," ,max energy is less than energy down limit,the max energy is: ",tempFloat," and energy down limit is: ",HydroEnergyLimitDown(hdp),/;
                      endif;
                    
                      if(tempFloat1>HydroEnergyLimit(hdp)) then
                        IsOpt:=0;
                        put Formatstring("Fatal Error!! HydroPlant %e",hdp)," ,min energy is exceed energy up limit HydroEnergyLimit,the min energy is: ",tempFloat1," and up limit is: ",HydroEnergyLimit(hdp),/;
                      endif;
                    endfor;
                    
                    
                    for i do
                            if CostBlockStart(i,Element(CostBlockSet,1),Element(Periods,2))>Reg_Pmin(i) then
                               IsOpt:=0;
                               put Formatstring("Error!!   %e",i)," ,start cost block power  is bigger than the Reg_Pmin",/;
                            endif;
                    
                            if CostBlockEnd(i,Element(CostBlockSet,NS),Element(Periods,2))<Reg_Pmax(i) then!xuebike edit 20150520
                               !IsOpt:=0;
                               put Formatstring("Error!!   %e",i)," ,end cost block power  is less than the Reg_Pmax",/;
                            endif;
                    endfor;
                    
                    for (i,l)|l>Element(CostBlockSet,1) do
                            if CostBlockStart(i,l,Element(Periods,2))<CostBlockEnd(i,l-1,Element(Periods,2)) then
                               IsOpt:=0;
                               put Formatstring("Error!!   %e",i)," ,the  cost block start power  is less than the previous block end power",/;
                            endif;
                    endfor;
                    
                    for (i,l) do
                            if CostBlockStart(i,l,Element(Periods,2))>CostBlockEnd(i,l,Element(Periods,2)) then
                               IsOpt:=0;
                               put Formatstring("Error!!   %e",i)," ,the  cost block start power  is large than the  block end power",/;
                            endif;
                    
                            if CostBlockEnd(i,l,Element(Periods,2))=0 then
                               IsOpt:=0;
                               put Formatstring("Error!!   %e",i)," ,the  cost block start power  and the  block end power is zero",/;
                            endif;
                    endfor;
                    
                    !!**************xuebike added at 20160127 for check bid data!!!
                    for (i,l,t) do
                    	if(UnitIncCost(i,l,t)<0)then
                    		IsOpt:=0;
                    		put Formatstring("Fatal Error!! %e %e %e",i,l,t)," ,the  UnitIncCost is less than zero the UnitIncCost is",UnitIncCost(i,l,t),/;
                    	endif;
                    endfor;
                    
                    for t|t>=element(Periods,2) do
                    	for (i,l)|l>Element(CostBlockSet,1) do
                    		if (UnitIncCost(i,l,t)< UnitIncCost(i,l-1,t)) then
                    		IsOpt:=0;
                    		put Formatstring("Error!!  UnitIncCost(%e,%e,%e)",i,l,t)," is less than ",FormatString("UnitIncCost(%e,%e,%e)",i,l-1,t);
                    		put Formatstring(" and UnitIncCost(%e,%e,%e)",i,l,t)," is ",UnitIncCost(i,l,t)," ",FormatString("UnitIncCost(%e,%e,%e)",i,l-1,t),"is ",UnitIncCost(i,l-1,t),/;
                    		endif;
                    	endfor;
                    endfor;
                    
                    
                    for t do
                    	tempFloat:=0;
                    	tempFloat1:=0;
                    	for i do
                    		tempFloat:=tempFloat + CostBlockStart(i,first(CostBlockSet),t)+sum [l, ( CostBlockEnd(i,l,t) - CostBlockStart(i,l,t) )];
                    	endfor;
                    
                    	for tie do
                           		tempFloat1:=tempFloat1 + TieLineFixedP(tie,t)*tieline_fix_direction(tie,t);
                      	endfor;
                      	tempFloat1:=tempFloat1+Load(t);
                    
                      	if(tempFloat<tempFloat1) then
                      		IsOpt:=0;
                      		put Formatstring("Fatal Error!! %e ",t)," ,the sum of all units bid block can't satisfy the load !! the sum of all units bid Block  is",tempFloat ," and the load plus the tieline fix power is ",tempFloat1,/;
                      	endif;
                    endfor;
                    !!**************endof xuebike added at 20160127 for check bid data!!!
                    
                    for tie do
                       for t do
                          if(TieLineFixedP(tie,t)>tiePmax(tie)) then
                             IsOpt:=0;
                             put formatstring("Error,the fixPower exceeds the PmaxLimit! %e",tie)," ",load_time(t)," , The tie fixed power is",TieLineFixedP(tie,t),",and the maximum tie power is",tiePmax(tie),/;
                          endif;
                    
                          if(TieLineFixedP(tie,t)<tiePmin(tie))then
                            IsOpt:=0;
                            put formatstring("Error,the fixPower exceeds the PminLimit! ! %e",tie)," ",load_time(t)," , The tie fixed power is",TieLineFixedP(tie,t),",and the minimum tie power is",tiePmin(tie),/;
                          endif;
                    
                       endfor;
                    endfor;
                    
                    for t do
                      tempFloat:=0;
                      for tie do
                           tempFloat:=tempFloat + TieLineFixedP(tie,t)*tieline_fix_direction(tie,t);
                      endfor;
                    
                      for i do
                         if ThermalOS_IsExist_Pmax_Temp(i,t) = 1 then
                           tempFloat:=tempFloat + ThermalOS_Pmax_Temp(i,t);
                         else
                           tempFloat:=tempFloat + Pmax(i,t);
                         endif;
                      endfor;
                    
                      if(tempFloat<Load(t)) then
                         put formatstring("Error,Tie Fix Power and All Unit MaxP can not supply the load")," ",load_time(t),",total supply is: ",tempFloat,",and the load is ",Load(t),/;
                      endif;
                    endfor;
                    
                    for t do
                      tempFloat:=0;
                      for tie do
                           tempFloat:=tempFloat + TieLineFixedP(tie,t)*tieline_fix_direction(tie,t);
                      endfor;
                    
                      for i do
                            if((i,t) in FixedOnOffSet) then
                              if ThermalOS_IsExist_Pmax_Temp(i,t) = 1 then
                              	tempFloat:=tempFloat+ThermalOS_Pmin_Temp(i,t)*FixedOnOffList(i,t);
                              else
                              	tempFloat:=tempFloat+Pmin(i,t)*FixedOnOffList(i,t);
                              endif;
                    
                            endif;
                      endfor;
                      if(tempFloat>Load(t)) then
                         IsOpt:=0;
                         put formatstring("Error,Tie Fix Power plus FixOn unit exceed the load")," ",load_time(t),",total supply is:",tempFloat," ,and the load is ",Load(t),/;
                      endif;
                    endfor;
                    
                    for t do
                      tempFloat:=0;
                      for tie do
                        tempFloat:=tempFloat + TieLineFixedP(tie,t)*tieline_fix_direction(tie,t);
                      endfor;
                    
                      for i|(i,t) in FixedScheduleSet do
                         tempFloat:=tempFloat + FixedOutPutPower(i,t);
                      endfor;
                    
                      if(tempFloat>Load(t)) then
                         IsOpt:=0;
                         put formatstring("Error,Tie Fix Power and unit FixPower exceed the load")," ",load_time(t),",total supply is: ",tempFloat,",and the load is ",Load(t),/;
                      endif;
                    endfor;
                    
                    for t|t>=element(Periods,2) do !xuebike edit 20150520
                      tempFloat:=0;
                      for tie do
                        tempFloat:=tempFloat+TieLineFixedP(tie,t)*tieline_fix_direction(tie,t);
                      endfor;
                    
                      for i do
                        if(t<=element( Periods,(1+ UTi(i) ))) then
                             if ThermalOS_IsExist_Pmax_Temp(i,t) = 1 then
                              	tempFloat:=tempFloat+ThermalOS_Pmin_Temp(i,t);
                             else
                           		tempFloat:=tempFloat +Reg_Pmin(i);
                           	 endif;
                        endif;
                    
                      endfor;
                    
                      if(tempFloat>Load(t)) then
                         IsOpt:=0;
                         put formatstring("Error,Tie Fix Power and MustRun Unit Power exceed the load")," ",load_time(t),",total supply is: ",tempFloat,",and the load is ",Load(t),/;
                      endif;
                    endfor;
                    
                    for t do!xuebike edit 20150520
                       tempFloat:=0;
                       for tie do
                         tempFloat:=tempFloat + TieLineFixedP(tie,t)*tieline_fix_direction(tie,t);
                       endfor;
                    
                       for i do
                         if((i,t) in FixedScheduleSet) then
                            tempFloat:=tempFloat + FixedOutPutPower(i,t);
                         elseif((i,t)in FixedOnOffSet)then
                             if ThermalOS_IsExist_Pmax_Temp(i,t) = 1 then
                              	tempFloat:=tempFloat+FixedOnOffList(i,t)*ThermalOS_Pmax_Temp(i,t);
                             else
                         		tempFloat:=tempFloat+FixedOnOffList(i,t)*Reg_Pmax(i);
                         	 endif;
                         else
                        	  if ThermalOS_IsExist_Pmax_Temp(i,t) = 1 then
                              	tempFloat:=tempFloat+ThermalOS_Pmax_Temp(i,t);
                              else
                            	tempFloat:=tempFloat + Reg_Pmax(i);
                              endif;
                         endif;
                       endfor;
                    
                      if(tempFloat<Load(t)) then
                        IsOpt:=0;
                         put formatstring("Error,Tie Fix Power plus unit MaxPower(FixPower) less than the load")," ",load_time(t),",total supply is: ",tempFloat,",and the load is ",Load(t),/;
                      endif;
                    
                    endfor;
                    
                    
                    for i do !!******************xuebike edit 20150520
                      for t|t<=element( Periods,(1+ UTi(i) )) and t>=element(Periods,2) do
                         if((i,t) in FixedScheduleSet) then
                            if(InitStatus(i)=1 and FixedOutPutPower(i,t) <=0)then
                                    IsOpt:=0;
                                    Put FormatString("Fatal Error: %e, %e",i,t)," ,The Given FixPower violate the InitialRunConstriant!!!!!!"/;
                            endif;
                         endif;
                      endfor;
                    endfor;
                    
                    for i do !!******************xuebike edit 20150520
                      for t|t<=element( Periods,(1+ DTi(i) )) and t>=element(Periods,2) do
                         if((i,t) in FixedScheduleSet) then
                            if(InitStatus(i)=0 and FixedOutPutPower(i,t) >0)then
                                    IsOpt:=0;
                                    Put FormatString("Fatal Error: %e, %e",i,t)," ,The Given FixPower violate the InitialOffConstriant!!!!!!"/;
                            endif;
                         endif;
                      endfor;
                    endfor;
                    
                    for t|t>=element(Periods,2) do !xuebike edit 20150520
                      tempFloat:=0;
                      for tie do
                        tempFloat:=tempFloat+TieLineFixedP(tie,t)*tieline_fix_direction(tie,t);
                      endfor;
                    
                      for i do
                        if((i,t) in FixedScheduleSet) then
                          tempFloat:=tempFloat + FixedOutPutPower(i,t);
                        endif;
                        if((not (i,t)in FixedScheduleSet) and InitStatus(i)=1 and t<=element( Periods,(1+ UTi(i) )))then
                        	  if ThermalOS_IsExist_Pmax_Temp(i,t) = 1 then
                              	tempFloat:=tempFloat+ThermalOS_Pmin_Temp(i,t);
                              else
                           		tempFloat:=tempFloat +Reg_Pmin(i);
                           	  endif;
                        endif;
                    
                      endfor;
                      if(tempFloat>Load(t)) then
                         IsOpt:=0;
                         put formatstring("Error,Tie Fix Power Plus FixPower and MustRun Unit Power exceed the load")," ",load_time(t),",total supply is: ",tempFloat,",and the load is ",Load(t),/;
                      endif;
                    endfor;
                    
                    for i do!xuebike edit 20150520
                      for t do
                         tempFloat:=CostBlockStart(i,first(CostBlockSet),t);
                         for l do
                            tempFloat:=tempFloat+ CostBlockEnd(i,l,t) - CostBlockStart(i,l,t);
                         endfor;
                         if((i,t) in FixedScheduleSet) then
                            if(tempFloat <FixedOutPutPower(i,t)) then
                              IsOpt:=0;
                              put formatstring("Error,the Cost Curve Segment total power  is less than FixPower! %e,%e",i,t)," , The total power is",tempFloat,",and the unit fix power is",FixedOutPutPower(i,t),/;
                            endif;
                         endif;
                      endfor;
                    endfor;
                    
                    for i do!xuebike edit 20150520
                       if Reg_PMin(i)<0 then
                          IsOpt:=0;
                           put formatstring("Fatal Error, Reg_PMin<0 ! %e",i)," ,Reg_PMin is:",Reg_PMin(i),/;
                       endif;
                    
                       if Reg_Pmax(i)<0 then
                           IsOpt:=0;
                           put formatstring("Fatal Error, Reg_Pmax<0 ! %e",i)," ,Reg_Pmax is:",Reg_Pmax(i),/;
                       endif;
                    
                       if Capacity(i)<0 then
                           IsOpt:=0;
                           put formatstring("Fatal Error, Capacity<0 ! %e",i)," ,Capacity is:",Capacity(i),/;
                       endif;
                       if RampUp(i)<0 then
                           IsOpt:=0;
                           put formatstring("Fatal Error, RampUp<0 ! %e",i)," ,RampUp is:",RampUp(i),/;
                       endif;
                       if RampDown(i)<0 then
                          IsOpt:=0;
                           put formatstring("Fatal Error, RampDown<0 ! %e",i)," ,RampDown is:",RampDown(i),/;
                       endif;
                    
                       if (Capacity(i)<Reg_PMin(i) or Capacity(i)>Reg_PMax(i)) then
                    
                           put formatstring("Fatal Error, Capacity is not between Reg_PMin and Reg_PMax! %e",i)," ,Capacity is:",Capacity(i),"Reg_PMin is:",Reg_PMin(i),"Reg_PMax is:",Reg_PMax(i),/;
                       endif;
                    
                    endfor;
                    
                    
                    for (i,t)|ThermalOS_IsExist_Pmax_Temp(i,t) = 1 do
                      if ThermalOS_Pmax_Temp(i,t)>Reg_Pmax(i) then
                         put Formatstring("Error!! unit  %e",i)," ",load_time(t)," ,ThermalOS_Pmax_Temp is bigger than Reg_Pmax,ThermalOS_Pmax_Temp is ",ThermalOS_Pmax_Temp(i,t)," Reg_Pmax is ",Reg_Pmax(i),/;
                      endif;
                    
                      if ThermalOS_Pmin_Temp(i,t)>=ThermalOS_Pmax_Temp(i,t) and ThermalOS_Pmin_Temp(i,t)>0 then
                         put Formatstring("Error!! unit  %e",i)," ",load_time(t)," ,ThermalOS_Pmin_Temp is bigger than ThermalOS_Pmax_Temp,ThermalOS_Pmin_Temp is ",ThermalOS_Pmin_Temp(i,t)," ThermalOS_Pmax_Temp is ",ThermalOS_Pmax_Temp(i,t),/;
                      endif;
                    endfor;
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    if UnitCostNum<=0 then
                    
                       put Formatstring("Error!! Unit Cost Segment num is Zero,UnitCostNum is "),UnitCostNum,/;
                    endif ;
                    
                    putclose;
                    
                    
                    !**************** warnning information ********************
                    put Warning_Infromation_file;
                    Warning_Infromation_file.pagewidth := 5000;
                    put "******************** !!! Warnning Information !!!!!!!!!!!!!!!***********************",/;
                    
                    ! ******************* Check the Load data **********************
                    for t | t >  'period-1' do
                            if abs(load(t) - load(t-1)) > load(t)*0.1 then
                                    put "The load of system at ",load_time(t)," is ",load(t)," and that at ", load_time(t-1)," is ",load(t-1),". The bias is ",abs(load(t)-load(t-1)),/;
                                    put "The load of system at ",load_time(t), " multiply 0.1 equal to ",load(t)*0.1,/;
                                    put load(t) - load(t-1)," > ",load(t)*0.1,/;
                            endif;
                    endfor;
                    putclose;
                }
            }
            Procedure Calculate_ccu_sens {
                Body: {
                    AS_CCUSens(ccu,m,nfg,t) := 0 ;
                    
                    for(ccu,m,nfg,t) do
                    
                            for(gst) do
                    
                                    if( CCUMemberList(ccu,gst) = 1 and  NFGSens(gst,nfg,t) > 0.000001 ) then
                    
                                            AS_CCUSens(ccu,m,nfg,t) := NFGSens(gst,nfg,t) ;
                    
                                            break ;
                                    endif ;
                    
                            endfor ;
                    
                    endfor ;
                }
            }
            Procedure Calculate_ccu_gfg_sens {
                Body: {
                    AS_CCU_gfg_sens(ccu,m,gfg) := 0 ;
                    
                    for(ccu,m,gfg) do
                    
                            for(gst) do
                    
                                    if( CCUMemberList(ccu,gst) = 1 and  GFGSens(gst,gfg) > 0.000001 ) then
                    
                                            AS_CCU_gfg_sens(ccu,m,gfg) := GFGSens(gst,gfg) ;
                    
                                            break ;
                                    endif ;
                    
                            endfor ;
                    
                    endfor ;
                }
            }
            Section MathmeticModel {
                DeclarationSection SystemBalance {
                    Constraint LoadBalanceConstraint {
                        IndexDomain: t;
                        Definition: {
                            !sum[(ccu,m), mP(ccu,m,t) ]
                            
                            ! C.H.H 2012-10-10
                            sum[i, Pi(i,t)]
                            /*+
                            sum[(ccu,m) , mP(ccu,m,t) ]
                            
                            */
                            +sum[tie , tieline_fix_direction(tie,t)*tieP(tie,t)]
                            
                            
                            = Load(t)
                        }
                    }
                    Constraint ReserveConstraint {
                        IndexDomain: (t);
                        Definition: {
                            Rsv(t) >= Reserve_Up(t)
                            !+sum[wd,Pi(wd,t)]
                            !+ ExpectedWindPower(t) !xuebike added at 2013.8.18.Additional resever for wind with value of the wind forecast power.
                            !+ ExpectedWindPower(t)-sum[wd,Pi(wd,t)]!xuebike added at 2013.8.18.Additional resever for wind with value of the deviation between the forecasting value and the real wind power.
                            
                            !+ 0.2*sum[wd,Pi(wd,t)] !!xuebike added at 2013.8.15. Additional resever for wind with value of the real wind power.
                        }
                    }
                    Constraint ReserveNegConstraint {
                        IndexDomain: (t);
                        Definition: RsvNeg(t) >= Reserve_Down(t);
                    }
                    Variable Rsv {
                        IndexDomain: (t);
                        Definition: {
                            sum[rsvUnit,Ui(rsvUnit,t)*Pmax(rsvUnit,t) - Pi(rsvUnit,t)]
                            !sum[i, Ui(i,t)*Pmax(i,t) - Pi(i,t)]
                            !+sum[(ccu,m) , Uc(ccu,m,t)*mPmax(ccu,m,t) - mP(ccu,m,t)] !xuebike 2013.01.23
                            
                            ! tieline reserver        GJ: 2009-9-18
                        }
                    }
                    Variable RsvNeg {
                        IndexDomain: (t);
                        Definition: {
                            sum[rsvUnit, Pi(rsvUnit,t) - Pmin(rsvUnit,t)*Ui(rsvUnit,t)]
                            !sum[i, Pi(i,t) - Ui(i,t)*Pmin(i,t)]
                            !+sum[(ccu,m) , mP(ccu,m,t) - Uc(ccu,m,t)*mPmin(ccu,m,t)]
                            
                            ! tieline reserver        GJ: 2009-9-18
                        }
                    }
                }
                DeclarationSection NetworkConstraints {
                    Variable NFGLimitRelax_up {
                        IndexDomain: (nfg,t);
                        Range: nonnegative;
                        Definition: {
                            !xuebike edit 20150422
                        }
                    }
                    Variable NFGLimitRelax_down {
                        IndexDomain: (nfg,t);
                        Range: nonnegative;
                        Comment: {
                            "!xuebike edit 20150422"
                        }
                    }
                    Parameter NFGLimitRelaxPunishCoeff {
                        IndexDomain: nfg;
                        Range: nonnegative;
                    }
                    Parameter AS_CCUSens {
                        IndexDomain: (ccu,m,nfg,t);
                    }
                    Constraint NormalFlowGateConstraints {
                        IndexDomain: (nfg,t);
                        Definition: {
                            !sum[i|abs(NFGSens(i,nfg,t))>0.0, NFGSens(i,nfg,t)* Pi(i,t) ] <= NFGLimit(nfg,t)
                            
                            !sum[i, NFGSens(i,nfg,t)* Pi(i,t) ] + NFGLoad(nfg,t) <= NFGLimit(nfg,t)
                            
                            sum[i, NFGSens(i,nfg,t)* Pi(i,t) ] + sum[tie, NFGSens(tie,nfg,t)*tieP(tie,t)*tieline_fix_direction(tie,t)]+NFGLoad(nfg,t) !xuebike edit 20150422
                            + sum[ (ccu,m) , mP(ccu,m,t)*AS_CCUSens(ccu,m,nfg,t) ]
                            <=
                            NFGLimit(nfg,t)+NFGLimitRelax_up(nfg,t)  !xuebike edit 20150422
                            
                            !when calculate tieline sens,tie power reference direction : power out is positive,power in is negative;
                            !                     and nfgload=sum[load_sense*load], and when calculate load sense power out is positive;
                            !when calculate generation unit sens,unit power reference direction: power in  is positive.
                        }
                    }
                    Constraint NFGCons {
                        IndexDomain: (nfg,t);
                        Definition: {
                            !sum[i, NFGSens(i,nfg,t)* Pi(i,t) ] + NFGLoad(nfg,t) >= -NFGLimit(nfg,t)
                            
                            sum[i, NFGSens(i,nfg,t)* Pi(i,t) ]+ sum[tie, NFGSens(tie,nfg,t)*tieP(tie,t)*tieline_fix_direction(tie,t)] + NFGLoad(nfg,t)!xuebike edit 20150422
                            + sum[ (ccu,m) , mP(ccu,m,t)*AS_CCUSens(ccu,m,nfg,t) ]
                            >= -NFGLimit(nfg,t)-NFGLimitRelax_down(nfg,t)  !xuebike edit 20150422
                        }
                    }
                    Parameter nfg_flow {
                        IndexDomain: (nfg,t);
                        Definition: sum[i, NFGSens(i,nfg,t)* Pi(i,t) ] + NFGLoad(nfg,t);
                    }
                    Parameter AS_CCU_gfg_sens {
                        IndexDomain: (ccu,m,gfg);
                    }
                    Constraint GeneratedFlowGateConstraints {
                        IndexDomain: (gfg);
                        Definition: {
                            !sum[i, GFGSens(i,gfg) * Pi(i, Element(Periods, GFGPeriodNo(gfg)+1) ) ] <= GFGLimit(gfg)
                            
                            !sum[i, GFGSens(i,gfg) * Pi(i, Element(Periods, GFGPeriodNo(gfg)+1) ) ] + GFGLoad(gfg) <= GFGLimit(gfg)
                            
                            sum[i, GFGSens(i,gfg) * Pi(i, Element(Periods, GFGPeriodNo(gfg)+1) ) ]
                            +sum[tie,GFGSens(tie,gfg)*TieP(tie,Element(Periods, GFGPeriodNo(gfg)+1) ) ]
                            +sum[(ccu,m) , mP(ccu,m,Element(Periods, GFGPeriodNo(gfg)+1))*AS_CCU_gfg_sens(ccu,m,gfg)]
                            
                            + GFGLoad(gfg) <= GFGLimit(gfg)
                        }
                    }
                    Constraint GFGCons {
                        IndexDomain: (gfg);
                        Definition: {
                            !sum[i, GFGSens(i,gfg) * Pi(i, Element(Periods, GFGPeriodNo(gfg)+1) ) ] + GFGLoad(gfg) >= -GFGLimit(gfg)
                            
                            sum[i, GFGSens(i,gfg) * Pi(i, Element(Periods, GFGPeriodNo(gfg)+1) ) ]
                            +sum[tie,GFGSens(tie,gfg)*TieP(tie,Element(Periods, GFGPeriodNo(gfg)+1) ) ]
                            +sum[(ccu,m) , mP(ccu,m,Element(Periods, GFGPeriodNo(gfg)+1))*AS_CCU_gfg_sens(ccu,m,gfg)]
                            
                            + GFGLoad(gfg) >= -GFGLimit(gfg)
                        }
                    }
                    Parameter gfg_flow {
                        IndexDomain: (gfg);
                        Definition: sum[i, GFGSens(i,gfg) * Pi(i, Element(Periods, GFGPeriodNo(gfg)+1) ) ] + GFGLoad(gfg);
                    }
                }
                DeclarationSection PlanOutageConstrains {
                    Constraint OutagePmaxPowerConstraints {
                        IndexDomain: (i,t) | ThermalOS_IsExist_Pmax_Temp(i,t) = 1;
                        Definition: {
                            Pi(i,t) <= ThermalOS_Pmax_Temp(i,t)*Ui(i,t)
                            !!comments by xuebike
                            !!The constraint is effective only to the thermal unit at special period
                            !!which satisfy the condition "ThermalOS_IsExist_Pmax_Temp(i,t) = 1".
                            !!And ThermalOS_Pmax_Temp(i,t) is the parameter that is initialized in the
                            !!procedure ThermalOS_UnitPowerLimitTemp_Init.
                        }
                    }
                    Constraint OutagePminPowerConstraints {
                        IndexDomain: (i,t) | ThermalOS_IsExist_Pmax_Temp(i,t) = 1;
                        Definition: {
                            Pi(i,t) >= ThermalOS_Pmin_Temp(i,t)*Ui(i,t)
                            !!The constraint is effective only to the thermal unit at special period
                            !!which satisfy the condition "ThermalOS_IsExist_Pmax_Temp(i,t) = 1"
                            !!And ThermalOS_Pmin_Temp(i,t) is the parameter that is initialized in the
                            !!procedure ThermalOS_UnitPowerLimitTemp_Init.
                        }
                    }
                }
                Section ThermalUnitSolution {
                    DeclarationSection Tunit3ModeStartup {
                        Index wt0 {
                            Range: Periods;
                        }
                        Index wt {
                            Range: Periods;
                        }
                        Index ct {
                            Range: Periods;
                        }
                        Index ct0 {
                            Range: Periods;
                            Comment: {
                                "!! assistant index"
                            }
                        }
                        Parameter s_ctc {
                            IndexDomain: (i);
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: {
                                max(   0,  min ( NT,  (  TimeToCold(i)-InitOffTime(i) )  )    )
                                !!comment by xuebike
                                !!cold-starting start time.
                            }
                        }
                        Parameter e_ctc {
                            IndexDomain: (i);
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: {
                                max(   0,  min ( NT,  TimeToCold(i)  )  )
                                !!comment by xuebike
                                !!cold-starting end time.
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint InitColdStartCostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t) | t>element(Periods, s_ctc(i)+1) and t<=element(periods,e_ctc(i)+1);
                            Definition: {
                                Si(i,t) >= ColdStartCost(i) * [ Ui(i,t) - sum ( ct0| ct0 >= First(Periods) and ct0<=t-1, Ui(i,ct0) )]
                                
                                !! s_ctc(i) is unit i cold-starting start time
                                !! e_ctc(i) is unit i cold-starting end time.
                                !! sum ( ct0| ct0 >= First(Periods) and ct0<=t-1, Ui(i,ct0) ) means
                                !! adding  the Ui the between the first element in set Period and current time t.
                                !! Before one unit finish starting ,the Ui is 0.If the unit is in process of starting ,the Ui is 0.
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint ColdStartCostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t) | t>element(Periods,e_CTC(i)+1);
                            Definition: {
                                Si(i,t) >= ColdStartCost(i) * [ Ui(i,t) - sum ( ct| ct >= t- TimeToCold(i) and ct<=t-1, Ui(i,ct) )]
                                !! e_ctc(i) is unit i cold-starting end time.
                                !! sum ( ct| ct >= t- TimeToCold(i) and ct<=t-1, Ui(i,ct) ) means
                                !! adding  the Ui the between the cold-starting end time and current time t.
                                !! Before one unit finish starting ,the Ui is 0.If the unit is in process of starting ,the Ui is 0.
                                !! ??????????????????????
                            }
                        }
                        Parameter s_wtc {
                            IndexDomain: (i);
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: {
                                max(   0,  min ( NT,  (  TimeToWarm(i)-InitOffTime(i) )  )    )
                                !!comment by xuebike
                                !!warm-starting start time.
                            }
                        }
                        Parameter e_wtc {
                            IndexDomain: (i);
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: {
                                max(   0,  min ( NT,  TimeToWarm(i)  )  )
                                !!comment by xuebike
                                !!warm-starting end time.
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint InitWarmStartCostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t) | t>element(Periods, s_wtc(i)+1) and t<=element(periods,e_wtc(i)+1);
                            Definition: Si(i,t) >= WarmStartCost(i) * [ Ui(i,t) - sum ( wt0| wt0 >= First(Periods) and wt0<=t-1, Ui(i,wt0) )];
                        }
                        Constraint WarmStartCostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t) |t>element(Periods,e_wtc(i)+1);
                            Definition: {
                                Si(i,t) >= WarmStartCost(i) * [ Ui(i,t) - sum ( wt| wt >= t- TimeToWarm(i) and wt<=t-1, Ui(i,wt) )]
                                !! e_wtc(i) is unit i warm-starting end time.
                                !! sum ( ct| ct >= t- TimeToWarm(i) and ct<=t-1, Ui(i,ct) ) means
                                !! adding  the Ui the between the warm-starting end time and current time t.
                                !! Before one unit finish starting ,the Ui is 0.If the unit is in process of starting ,the Ui is 0.
                                !! ??????????????????????
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint HotStartCostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t);
                            Definition: Si(i,t) >= HotStartCost(i) * [ Ui(i,t) - Ui(i,t-1)];
                        }
                    }
                    DeclarationSection TUnitModel {
                        Variable Ci {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t);
                            Definition: {
                                 !! GengJian TEST 2008-10-28
                                /*
                                Pi(i,t)*UnitCost(i,First(CostBlockSet))
                                */
                                
                                !( Ui(i,t)* UnitBaseCost(i,first(CostBlockSet),t) + sum[l, UnitIncCost(i,l,t)*pli(i,l,t)] ) *PrdMin/60
                                ( Ui(i,t)* UnitBaseCost(i,first(CostBlockSet),t) + sum[l, GenAdjustedBidPrice(i,l,t)*pli(i,l,t)] ) *PrdMin/60
                            }
                        }
                        Variable Pi {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t);
                            Range: nonnegative;
                            Definition: Ui(i,t)*CostBlockStart(i,first(CostBlockSet),t)+ sum [l, pli(i,l,t)];
                        }
                        Variable pli {
                            IndexDomain: (i,l,t);
                            Range: nonnegative;
                            Definition: {
                                !!this is UCVariable
                            }
                        }
                        Variable Si {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t);
                            Range: nonnegative;
                            Definition: {
                                !yi(i,t)*ColdStartCost(i)
                                
                                !!Following comments by xuebike
                                !!Si is the unit start cost.
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint pliConstraint2 {
                            IndexDomain: (i,l,t);
                            Definition: pli(i,l,t) <= ( CostBlockEnd(i,l,t) - CostBlockStart(i,l,t) );
                        }
                        Constraint SiConsXF {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t);
                            Definition: Si(i,t) >= ColdStartCost(i) * ( Ui(i,t) - Ui(i,t-1) );
                        }
                        Constraint SiConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t);
                            Definition: {
                                !!Si(i,t) = yi(i,t)*ColdStartCost(i)
                                
                                Si(i,t) = yi(i,t)*Time_ColdStartCost(i,t)
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    DeclarationSection TUnit_StatusConstraints {
                        Variable Ui {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t);
                            Range: binary;
                        }
                        Constraint pliConstraint1 {
                            IndexDomain: (i,l,t);
                            Definition: {
                                pli(i,l,t) >= 0
                                !!comment by xuebike
                                !!i->Thermal unit dimension
                                !!l->Thermal unit cost curve segment dimension
                                !!t->time dimension
                            }
                        }
                        Variable yi {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t);
                            Range: binary;
                        }
                        Variable zi {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t);
                            Range: binary;
                        }
                        Constraint yzConstraint1 {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t);
                            Definition: Ui(i,t)-Ui(i,t-1) = yi(i,t) - zi(i,t);
                        }
                        Constraint yzConstraint2 {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t);
                            Definition: yi(i,t) + zi(i,t) <= 1;
                        }
                    }
                    DeclarationSection TUnit_GeneralConstraints {
                        Constraint UnitMaxOutConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t);
                            Definition: Pi(i,t)<=Pmax(i,t)*Ui(i,t);
                        }
                        Constraint UnitMinOutConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t);
                            Definition: Pi(i,t)>=Pmin(i,t)*Ui(i,t);
                        }
                        Constraint UnitRampUpConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t);
                            Definition: {
                                !Pi(i,t)<=Pi(i,t-1)+RampUp(i)*PrdMin*Ui(i,t-1) + Pmax(i,t)*(1-Ui(i,t-1))
                                
                                Pi(i,t)<=Pi(i,t-1)+RampUp(i)*PrdMin*Ui(i,t-1) +Pmax(i,t)*(1-Ui(i,t-1))!xuebike edit 20150630
                                
                                !! comments by xuebike
                                !! PA PO constraint.
                                !! If the Ui(i,t-1)=1 ,that is :
                                !!      Pi(i,t)<=Pi(i,t-1)+RampUp(i)*PrdMin*Ui(i,t-1)
                                !!if the Ui(i,t-1)=0 ,that is:
                                !!      Pi(i,t)<=Pmin(i,t)
                                !! It seems there is some error, should Pmin be Pmax?
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint UnitRampDownConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t);
                            Definition: {
                                Pi(i,t-1) - Pi(i,t) <= RampDown(i)*PrdMin*Ui(i,t) +(1-Ui(i,t))*Pmax(i,t)
                                !Pi(i,t-1) - Pi(i,t) <= RampDown(i)*PrdMin*Ui(i,t) +(1-Ui(i,t))*Pmin(i,t)
                                
                                !!comments by xuebike
                                !!HUA PO constraint
                                !! It seems there is some error, should Pmax be Pmin?
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    DeclarationSection TUnit_MinOnConstraints {
                        Constraint InitUpConsXF {
                            IndexDomain: (i);
                            Definition: sum[t |t<=element( Periods,( 1+UTi(i) ) ), (1-Ui(i,t))] = 0;
                        }
                        Constraint MinUpConsXF {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t)|t>element(Periods,(1+UTi(i)))and t<=element(Periods,NT-MinOnTime(i)+2);
                            Definition: sum[j | j>=t and j<= element(Periods , ord(t,periods)+MinOnTime(i)-1) , Ui(i,j)] >= MinOnTime(i) * ( Ui(i,t) - Ui(i,t-1) );
                        }
                        Constraint FinalUpConsXF {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t)|t>element(Periods , NT-MinOnTime(i)+2);
                            Definition: sum[j|j>=t , Ui(i,j)- ( Ui(i,t) - Ui(i,t-1) )  ] >= 0;
                        }
                        Constraint InitDownConsXF {
                            IndexDomain: (i);
                            Definition: sum[t |t<=element( Periods,( 1+ DTi(i) ) ), Ui(i,t)] = 0;
                        }
                        Constraint MinDownConsXF {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t)|t>element(Periods,(1+DTi(i)))and t<=element(Periods,NT-MinOffTime(i)+2);
                            Definition: sum[k | k>=t and k<= element(Periods , ord(t,periods)+MinOffTime(i)-1) , ( 1 - Ui(i,k) ) ] >= MinOffTime(i) * ( Ui(i,t-1) - Ui(i,t) );
                        }
                        Constraint FinalDownConsXF {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t)|t>element(Periods , NT-MinOffTime(i)+2);
                            Definition: sum[k|k>=t , 1 - Ui(i,k) - ( Ui(i,t-1) - Ui(i,t) )  ] >= 0;
                        }
                        Parameter UTi {
                            IndexDomain: (i);
                            Range: nonnegative;
                            Definition: max(0,  min (NT,  ( MinOnTime(i)-InitOnTime(i) ) *InitStatus(i)  )  );
                        }
                        Constraint InitialRunConstriant {
                            IndexDomain: i;
                            Definition: {
                                sum[t | t<=element( Periods,(1+ UTi(i) ) ), (1-Ui(i,t))] = 0
                                
                                !sum[t |t>=element( Periods,( 2) ) and t<=element( Periods,(1+ UTi(i) ) ), (1-Ui(i,t))] = 0
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint UnitMinUpConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t)| t>element( Periods,( 1+UTi(i) ) );
                            Definition: yi(i,t) + sum[ j| j>=t+1 and j<= element(Periods, min(NT, Ord(t,periods)-1+MinOnTime(i)-1 )+1),zi(i,j)] <=1;
                        }
                        Index j {
                            Range: Periods;
                        }
                        Parameter DTi {
                            IndexDomain: (i);
                            Range: nonnegative;
                            Definition: max(   0,  min ( NT,  ( MinOffTime(i)-InitOffTime(i) ) *(1-InitStatus(i) ) )    );
                        }
                        Constraint InitialOffConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: i;
                            Definition: {
                                sum[t | t<=element( Periods,( 1+ DTi(i) ) ), Ui(i,t)] = 0
                                
                                !sum[t |t>=element( Periods,( 2 ) ) and t<=element( Periods,( 1+ DTi(i) ) ), Ui(i,t)] = 0
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint UnitMinDownConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t)|t>element( Periods,( 1+ DTi(i) ));
                            Definition: zi(i,t) + sum[ k| k>=t+1 and k<= element(Periods, min(NT, Ord(t,periods)-1+MinOffTime(i)-1 )+1 ),yi(i,k)] <=1;
                        }
                        Index k {
                            Range: Periods;
                        }
                    }
                }
                Section TieLineSolution {
                    DeclarationSection TieLineModel {
                        Variable tieP {
                            IndexDomain: (tie,t);
                            Range: nonnegative;
                        }
                        Variable tieCost {
                            IndexDomain: (tie,t);
                            Definition: {
                                !tieP(tie,t) * tiePrice(tie,t)*PrdMin/60
                                tieline_fix_direction(tie,t)*tieP(tie,t) * tiePrice(tie,t)*PrdMin/60!xuebike
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    DeclarationSection ItsConstraints {
                        Variable UnitTieP {
                            IndexDomain: (its,t);
                            Range: free;
                        }
                        Constraint ItsPmaxConstraints {
                            IndexDomain: (its,t) | (its,t) in ItsNormalLimitSet;
