                            Definition: sum[ tie|ItsTielineList(its,tie), tieP(tie,t)] <= ItsPmax(its,t);
                        }
                        Constraint ItsPminConstraints {
                            IndexDomain: (its,t) | (its,t) in ItsNormalLimitSet;
                            Definition: sum[ tie|ItsTielineList(its,tie), tieP(tie,t)] >= ItsPmin(its,t);
                        }
                        Constraint ItsPlanConstraints {
                            IndexDomain: (its,t);
                            Definition: sum[ tie|ItsTielineList(its,tie), tieP(tie,t)] = ItsPowerPlan(its,t);
                        }
                    }
                    DeclarationSection TieLine_PowerConstraints {
                        Constraint TiePRateConstraints {
                            IndexDomain: (its,tie,t) |ItsTielineList(its,tie);
                            Definition: tieP(tie,t) = UnitTieP(its,t) * TieIsRun(tie,t)* TieDecomRate(tie,t);
                        }
                        Constraint tieMaxOutCons {
                            IndexDomain: (tie,t);
                            Definition: {
                                tieP(tie,t) <= tiePmax(tie)
                                !tieP(tie,t) <= 99999999999.0
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint tieMinOutCons {
                            IndexDomain: (tie,t);
                            Definition: {
                                tieP(tie,t) >= tiePmin(tie)
                                !tieP(tie,t) >= -9999999999.9
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint TieLineFixedPowerCons {
                            IndexDomain: (tie,t) in TieLineFixedPowerSet;
                            Definition: tieP(tie,t) = TieLineFixedP(tie,t);
                        }
                    }
                }
                Section CCUSolution {
                    DeclarationSection CCUnitModel {
                        Variable mCost {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t);
                            Text: "COST FOR EACH MODE";
                            Definition: {
                                sum[
                                m,
                                
                                Uc(ccu,m,t) * ccuBaseCost(ccu,m,first(CostBlockSet),t)
                                +
                                sum[ l , mpx(ccu,m,l,t) * ccuIncCost(ccu,m,l,t) ]
                                
                                ]
                                *PrdMin/60
                            }
                        }
                        Variable ccuTCost {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t);
                        }
                        Variable mP {
                            IndexDomain: {
                                (ccu,m,t) !| val(m) <= NMode(ccu)
                            }
                            Text: "POWER FOR EACH MODE";
                            Range: nonnegative;
                            Definition: {
                                /*mPmin(ccu,m,t) * Uc(ccu,m,t)
                                +
                                sum[l , mpx(ccu,m,l,t) ]*/  !modified by ZYT 2010.6.8
                                
                                ccuCostBlockStart(ccu,m,first(CostBlockSet),t)* Uc(ccu,m,t) + sum[l , mpx(ccu,m,l,t) ]
                            }
                        }
                        Parameter ccuP {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t);
                            Text: "POWER FOR EACH CCU";
                            Definition: sum[m  , mP(ccu,m,t)];
                        }
                        Variable mpx {
                            IndexDomain: {
                                (ccu,m,l,t) ! | val(m) <= NMode(ccu)
                            }
                            Text: "POWER BLOCK FOR EACH MODE OF CCU";
                            Range: nonnegative;
                        }
                        Constraint mpxMaxCons {
                            IndexDomain: {
                                (ccu,m,l,t) !| val(m) <= NMode(ccu)
                            }
                            Definition: {
                                mpx(ccu,m,l,t)
                                <=
                                ccuCostBlockEnd(ccu,m,l,t) - ccuCostBlockStart(ccu,m,l,t)
                            }
                        }
                        Variable ccu4ModeTcost {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t);
                            Range: nonnegative;
                        }
                        Variable GTRunningCost {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,gt,d);
                            Range: nonnegative;
                            Definition: sum[t|element(Periods,(val(d)-1)*24*60/PrdMin + 2) <= t and t <= element(Periods,val(d)*24*60/PrdMin+1),ccu_ui(ccu,gt,t)*CCURunningCost(ccu,gt) - ProductLiner(ccu,gt,d,t)*CCURunningCost(ccu,gt) ]*PrdMin/60;
                        }
                        Variable ProductLiner {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,gt,d,t);
                        }
                        Variable CCUTotalRunningCost {
                            Definition: {
                                sum[(ccu,gt,d),GTRunningCost(ccu,gt,d)]
                                !+ sum[(ccu,st,d),STRunningCost(ccu,st,d)]
                            }
                        }
                        Variable IS_EsCostGT {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,gt,d);
                            Range: binary;
                        }
                        Variable Is_StRunning {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,st,d,t);
                            Range: binary;
                        }
                        Constraint Is_EsCostGT_Down {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,gt,d);
                            Definition: Is_EsCostGT(ccu,gt,d) <= sum[t|element(Periods,(val(d)-1)*(24*60/PrdMin) + 2) <= t and t <= element(Periods,val(d)*(24*60/PrdMin)+1),ccu_yi(ccu,gt,t)];
                        }
                        Constraint Is_EsCostGT_Up {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,gt,d);
                            Definition: sum[t|element(Periods,(val(d)-1)*(24*60/PrdMin) + 2) <= t and t <= element(Periods,val(d)*(24*60/PrdMin)+1),ccu_yi(ccu,gt,t)]  <=  Is_EsCostGT(ccu,gt,d)*(NT+1);
                        }
                        Constraint ProductLinearCostraint1 {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,gt,d,t) | element(Periods,(val(d)-1)*24*60/PrdMin + 2) <= t and t <= element(Periods,val(d)*24*60/PrdMin+1);
                            Definition: ProductLiner(ccu,gt,d,t) <= ccu_ui(ccu,gt,t);
                        }
                        Constraint ProductLinearConstraint2 {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,gt,d,t)  | element(Periods,(val(d)-1)*24*60/PrdMin + 2) <= t and t <= element(Periods,val(d)*24*60/PrdMin+1);
                            Definition: ProductLiner(ccu,gt,d,t) <= IS_EsCostGT(ccu,gt,d);
                        }
                        Constraint ProductLinearConstraint3 {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,gt,d,t)  | element(Periods,(val(d)-1)*24*60/PrdMin + 2) <= t and t <= element(Periods,val(d)*24*60/PrdMin+1);
                            Definition: ProductLiner(ccu,gt,d,t) >= IS_EsCostGT(ccu,gt,d) + ccu_ui(ccu,gt,t) - 1;
                        }
                        Constraint STRunningConstraintsUp {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,st,d,t);
                            Definition: Is_StRunning(ccu,st,d,t) <= ord(t,periods)-(val(d)-1)*24*60/prdmin -1 - sum[t1|element(periods,(val(d)-1)*24*60/prdmin-1) <= t1 and t1 <= t,ccu_ui(ccu,st,t1)];
                        }
                        Constraint STRunningConstraintsDown {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,st,d,t);
                            Definition: Is_StRunning(ccu,st,d,t)*NT >= ord(t-1,periods)-(val(d)-1)*24*60/prdmin -1 - sum[t1|element(periods,(val(d)-1)*24*60/prdmin-1) <= t1 and t1 <= t-1,ccu_ui(ccu,st,t1)];
                        }
                        Variable STRunningCost {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,st,d);
                            Definition: sum[t|element(Periods,(val(d)-1)*24*60/PrdMin + 2) <= t and t <= element(Periods,val(d)*24*60/PrdMin+1),(1-Is_StRunning(ccu,st,d,t))*CCURunningCost(ccu,st)]*PrdMin/60;
                        }
                    }
                    DeclarationSection CCU_StatusConstraints {
                        Variable Uc {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m,t) | val(m) <= NMode(ccu);
                            Text: "UI FOR EACH MODE";
                            Range: binary;
                        }
                        Parameter Uccu {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t);
                            Text: "STATICS UI FOR EACH CCU";
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: {
                                sum[
                                m | m>'0' and val(m) <= NMode(ccu) ,
                                Uc(ccu,m,t)
                                ]
                            }
                        }
                        Variable yc {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m,t)| val(m) <= NMode(ccu);
                            Range: binary;
                        }
                        Variable zc {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m,t) | val(m) <= NMode(ccu);
                            Range: [0, 1];
                        }
                        Variable ccu_ui {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,gst,t);
                            Range: binary;
                            Definition: sum[m,Uc(ccu,m,t)*ModeGTList(ccu,m,gst)];
                        }
                        Variable ccu_yi {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,gt,t);
                            Range: binary;
                        }
                        Variable ccu_zi {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,gt,t);
                            Range: binary;
                        }
                        Constraint SingleModeCons {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t);
                            Definition: sum[m  , Uc(ccu,m,t) ] = 1;
                        }
                        Constraint ccu_yzCons1 {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m,t)| val(m) <= NMode(ccu);
                            Definition: yc(ccu,m,t) + zc(ccu,m,t) <= 1;
                        }
                        Constraint ccu_yzCons2 {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m,t)| val(m) <= NMode(ccu);
                            Definition: yc(ccu,m,t) - zc(ccu,m,t) = Uc(ccu,m,t) - Uc(ccu,m,t-1);
                        }
                        Constraint ccu_yizicons1 {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,gt,t);
                            Definition: ccu_yi(ccu,gt,t) + ccu_zi(ccu,gt,t) <= 1;
                        }
                        Constraint ccu_yizicons2 {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,gt,t);
                            Definition: ccu_ui(ccu,gt,t) - ccu_ui(ccu,gt,t-1) = ccu_yi(ccu,gt,t) - ccu_zi(ccu,gt,t);
                        }
                    }
                    DeclarationSection TransitionConstraints {
                        Constraint TransModeCons {
                            IndexDomain: {
                                (ccu,m,t) | val(m) <= NMode(ccu) ! and t>'Period-01'
                            }
                            Definition: {
                                1
                                -
                                sum[m2 , TransMatrix(ccu,m,m2) * Uc(ccu,m2,t) ]
                                +
                                sum[m2 , ( 1 - TransMatrix(ccu,m,m2) ) * Uc(ccu,m2,t) ]
                                <=
                                2 * ( 1 - Uc(ccu,m,t-1) )
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint TransFuelCons {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m,t);
                            Definition: {
                                ccuTCost(ccu,t) >=sum[m2 ,TransCost(ccu,m,m2) * ( Uc(ccu,m,t-1) + Uc(ccu,m2,t) - 1 )]
                                
                                !ccuTCost(ccu,t) =0.0
                                
                                !ccuTCost(ccu,t) >= sum[m2 ,Time_TransCost(ccu,m,m2,t) * ( Uc(ccu,m,t-1) + Uc(ccu,m2,t) - 1 )]
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint TransRUCons {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m,m2,t);
                            Definition: {
                                mP(ccu,m2,t) - mP(ccu,m,t-1)
                                <=
                                TransRU(ccu,m,m2)
                                +
                                CCUPmax(ccu) * ( 2 - Uc(ccu,m,t-1) - Uc(ccu,m2,t) )
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint TransRDCons {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m,m2,t);
                            Definition: {
                                mP(ccu,m,t-1) - mP(ccu,m2,t)
                                <=
                                TransRD(ccu,m,m2)
                                +
                                CCUPmax(ccu) * ( 2 - Uc(ccu,m,t-1) - Uc(ccu,m2,t) )
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    DeclarationSection CCU_GeneralConstraints {
                        Constraint ccuMaxOutCons {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m,t) | val(m) <= NMode(ccu);
                            Definition: mP(ccu,m,t) <= mPmax(ccu,m,t) * Uc(ccu,m,t);
                        }
                        Constraint ccuMinOutCons {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m,t)| val(m) <= NMode(ccu);
                            Definition: mP(ccu,m,t) >= mPmin(ccu,m,t) * Uc(ccu,m,t);
                        }
                        Constraint ccuRampUpCons {
                            IndexDomain: {
                                (ccu,m,t) | val(m) <= NMode(ccu) !and t>'Period-01'
                            }
                            Definition: mP(ccu,m,t) - mP(ccu,m,t-1) <= mRampUp(ccu,m)*PrdMin + mPmax(ccu,m,t)* ( 2 - Uc(ccu,m,t) - Uc(ccu,m,t-1) );
                        }
                        Constraint ccuRampDownCons {
                            IndexDomain: {
                                (ccu,m,t) | val(m) <= NMode(ccu)  ! and t>'Period-01'
                            }
                            Definition: mP(ccu,m,t-1) - mP(ccu,m,t) <= mRampDown(ccu,m)*PrdMin + mPmax(ccu,m,t)* ( 2 - Uc(ccu,m,t) - Uc(ccu,m,t-1) );
                        }
                    }
                    DeclarationSection CCU_MinOnConstraints {
                        Parameter ccuUT {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m);
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: max(0,  min (NT,  ( mMinOnTime(ccu,m)-mInitOnTime(ccu,m) ) *mInitStatus(ccu,m)  )  );
                        }
                        Index t2 {
                            Range: Periods;
                        }
                        Constraint ccuInitOnCons {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m);
                            Definition: sum[t |t<=element( Periods,( 1+ccuUT(ccu,m) ) ), (1-Uc(ccu,m,t))] = 0;
                        }
                        Constraint ccuMinOnCons {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m,t);
                            Definition: {
                                yc(ccu,m,t)
                                +
                                sum
                                [
                                 t2| t2>=t+1 and t2<= element(Periods, min(NT, Ord(t,periods)-1+mMinOnTime(ccu,m)-1 )+1),
                                 zc(ccu,m,t2)
                                ]
                                <=1
                            }
                        }
                        Parameter ccuDT {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m);
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: max(0,  min (NT,  ( mMinOffTime(ccu,m)-mInitOffTime(ccu,m) ) *(1-mInitStatus(ccu,m) ) )    );
                        }
                        Index t3 {
                            Range: Periods;
                        }
                        Constraint ccuInitOffCons {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m);
                            Definition: sum[t |t<=element( Periods,( 1+ccuDT(ccu,m) ) ), Uc(ccu,m,t)] = 0;
                        }
                        Constraint ccuMinOffCons {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m,t);
                            Definition: {
                                zc(ccu,m,t)
                                +
                                sum
                                [
                                 t3| t3>=t+1 and t3<= element(Periods, min(NT, Ord(t,periods)-1+mMinOffTime(ccu,m)-1 )+1 ),
                                 yc(ccu,m,t3)
                                ]
                                <=1
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    DeclarationSection CCUnit4ModeTansition {
                        Index ccu_wat0 {
                            Range: Periods;
                        }
                        Index ccu_wat {
                            Range: Periods;
                        }
                        Index ccu_wbt0 {
                            Range: Periods;
                        }
                        Index ccu_wbt {
                            Range: Periods;
                        }
                        Index ccu_ct {
                            Range: Periods;
                        }
                        Index ccu_ct0 {
                            Range: Periods;
                        }
                        Parameter ccu_s_1ctc4 {
                            IndexDomain: ccu;
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: max(   0,  min ( NT,  (  TransTimeToCold(ccu,'1','4')- min(mInitOffTime(ccu,'6'),mInitOffTime(ccu,'4') ) )  )    );
                        }
                        Parameter ccu_s_1wbtc4 {
                            IndexDomain: ccu;
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: max(   0,  min ( NT,  (  TransTimeToWarmB(ccu,'1','4')- min(mInitOffTime(ccu,'6'),mInitOffTime(ccu,'4') ) )  )    );
                        }
                        Parameter ccu_s_1watc4 {
                            IndexDomain: ccu;
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: max(   0,  min ( NT,  (  TransTimeToWarmA(ccu,'1','4')- min(mInitOffTime(ccu,'6'),mInitOffTime(ccu,'4') ) )  )    );
                        }
                        Parameter ccu_s_2ctc5 {
                            IndexDomain: ccu;
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: max(   0,  min ( NT,  (  TransTimeToCold(ccu,'2','5')- min(mInitOffTime(ccu,'6'),mInitOffTime(ccu,'5') ) )  )    );
                        }
                        Parameter ccu_s_2watc5 {
                            IndexDomain: ccu;
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: max(   0,  min ( NT,  (  TransTimeToWarmA(ccu,'2','5')- min(mInitOffTime(ccu,'6'),mInitOffTime(ccu,'5') ) )  )    );
                        }
                        Parameter ccu_s_2wbtc5 {
                            IndexDomain: ccu;
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: max(   0,  min ( NT,  (  TransTimeToWarmB(ccu,'2','5')- min(mInitOffTime(ccu,'6'),mInitOffTime(ccu,'5') ) )  )    );
                        }
                        Parameter ccu_s_4ctc6 {
                            IndexDomain: ccu;
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: max(   0,  min ( NT,  (  TransTimeToCold(ccu,'4','6')- min(mInitOffTime(ccu,'6'),mInitOffTime(ccu,'5') ) )  )    );
                        }
                        Parameter ccu_s_4watc6 {
                            IndexDomain: ccu;
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: max(   0,  min ( NT,  (  TransTimeToWarmA(ccu,'4','6')- min(mInitOffTime(ccu,'6'),mInitOffTime(ccu,'5') ) )  )    );
                        }
                        Parameter ccu_s_4wbtc6 {
                            IndexDomain: ccu;
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: max(   0,  min ( NT,  (  TransTimeToWarmB(ccu,'4','6')- min(mInitOffTime(ccu,'6'),mInitOffTime(ccu,'5') ) )  )    );
                        }
                        Parameter ccu_s_5ctc6 {
                            IndexDomain: ccu;
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: max(   0,  min ( NT,  (  TransTimeToCold(ccu,'5','6')- min(mInitOffTime(ccu,'6'),mInitOffTime(ccu,'4') ) )  )    );
                        }
                        Parameter ccu_s_5wbtc6 {
                            IndexDomain: ccu;
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: max(   0,  min ( NT,  (  TransTimeToWarmB(ccu,'5','6')- min(mInitOffTime(ccu,'6'),mInitOffTime(ccu,'4') ) )  )    );
                        }
                        Parameter ccu_s_5watc6 {
                            IndexDomain: ccu;
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: max(   0,  min ( NT,  (  TransTimeToWarmA(ccu,'5','6')- min(mInitOffTime(ccu,'6'),mInitOffTime(ccu,'4') ) )  )    );
                        }
                        Parameter ccu_e_ctc {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m,m2);
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: max(   0,  min ( NT,  TransTimeToCold(ccu,m,m2)  )  );
                        }
                        Parameter ccu_e_watc {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m,m2);
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: max(   0,  min ( NT,  TransTimeToWarmA(ccu,m,m2)  )  );
                        }
                        Parameter ccu_e_wbtc {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m,m2);
                            Range: integer;
                            Definition: max(   0,  min ( NT,  TransTimeToWarmB(ccu,m,m2)  )  );
                        }
                        Constraint InitCCUCold1Trans4CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t) | t>element(Periods, ccu_s_1ctc4(ccu)+1) and t<=element(periods,ccu_e_ctc(ccu,'1','4')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= ColdTransCost(ccu,'1','4')*(Uc(ccu,'4',t) - Sum[ccu_ct0 | ccu_ct0 >= First(Periods)
                                        and ccu_ct0 <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'4',ccu_ct0) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_ct0)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint InitCCUWarmA1Trans4CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t) | t>element(Periods, ccu_s_1watc4(ccu)+1) and t<=element(periods,ccu_e_watc(ccu,'1','4')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= WarmATransCost(ccu,'1','4')*(Uc(ccu,'4',t) - Sum[ccu_wat0 | ccu_wat0 >= First(Periods)
                                        and ccu_wat0 <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'4',ccu_wat0) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_wat0)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint InitCCUWarmB1Trans4CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t) | t>element(Periods, ccu_s_1wbtc4(ccu)+1) and t<=element(periods,ccu_e_wbtc(ccu,'1','4')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= WarmBTransCost(ccu,'1','4')*(Uc(ccu,'4',t) - Sum[ccu_wbt0 | ccu_wbt0 >= First(Periods)
                                        and ccu_wbt0 <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'4',ccu_wbt0) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_wbt0)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint CCUCold1Trans4CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t)| t>element(Periods,ccu_e_ctc(ccu,'1','4')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= ColdTransCost(ccu,'1','4')*(Uc(ccu,'4',t) - Sum[ccu_ct | ccu_ct >= t - TransTimeToCold(ccu,'1','4')
                                        and ccu_ct <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'4',ccu_ct) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_ct)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint CCUWarmA1Trans4CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t)| t>element(Periods,ccu_e_watc(ccu,'1','4')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= WarmATransCost(ccu,'1','4')*(Uc(ccu,'4',t) - Sum[ccu_wat | ccu_wat >= t - TransTimeToWarmA(ccu,'1','4')
                                        and ccu_wat <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'4',ccu_wat) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_wat)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint CCUWarmB1Trans4CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t)| t>element(Periods,ccu_e_wbtc(ccu,'1','4')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= WarmBTransCost(ccu,'1','4')*(Uc(ccu,'4',t) - Sum[ccu_wbt | ccu_wbt >= t - TransTimeToWarmB(ccu,'1','4')
                                        and ccu_wbt <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'4',ccu_wbt) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_wbt)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint InitCCUCold2Trans5CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t) | t>element(Periods, ccu_s_2ctc5(ccu)+1) and t<=element(periods,ccu_e_ctc(ccu,'2','5')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= ColdTransCost(ccu,'2','5')*(Uc(ccu,'5',t) - Sum[ccu_ct0 | ccu_ct0 >= First(Periods)
                                        and ccu_ct0 <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'5',ccu_ct0) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_ct0)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint InitCCUWarmA2Trans5CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t) | t>element(Periods, ccu_s_2watc5(ccu)+1) and t<=element(periods,ccu_e_watc(ccu,'2','5')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= WarmATransCost(ccu,'2','5')*(Uc(ccu,'5',t) - Sum[ccu_wat0 | ccu_wat0 >= First(Periods)
                                        and ccu_wat0 <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'5',ccu_wat0) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_wat0)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint InitCCUWarmB2Trans5CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t) | t>element(Periods, ccu_s_2wbtc5(ccu)+1) and t<=element(periods,ccu_e_wbtc(ccu,'2','5')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= WarmBTransCost(ccu,'2','5')*(Uc(ccu,'5',t) - Sum[ccu_wbt0 | ccu_wbt0 >= First(Periods)
                                        and ccu_wbt0 <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'5',ccu_wbt0) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_wbt0)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint CCUCold2Trans5CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t)| t>element(Periods,ccu_e_ctc(ccu,'2','5')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= ColdTransCost(ccu,'2','5')*(Uc(ccu,'5',t) - Sum[ccu_ct | ccu_ct >= t - TransTimeToCold(ccu,'2','5')
                                        and ccu_ct <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'5',ccu_ct) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_ct)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint CCUWarmA2Trans5CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t)| t>element(Periods,ccu_e_watc(ccu,'2','5')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= WarmATransCost(ccu,'2','5')*(Uc(ccu,'5',t) - Sum[ccu_wat | ccu_wat >= t - TransTimeToWarmA(ccu,'2','5')
                                        and ccu_wat <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'5',ccu_wat) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_wat)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint CCUWarmB2Trans5CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t)| t>element(Periods,ccu_e_wbtc(ccu,'2','5')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= WarmBTransCost(ccu,'2','5')*(Uc(ccu,'5',t) - Sum[ccu_wbt | ccu_wbt >= t - TransTimeToWarmB(ccu,'2','5')
                                        and ccu_wbt <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'5',ccu_wbt) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_wbt)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint InitCCUCold4Trans6CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t) | t>element(Periods, ccu_s_4ctc6(ccu)+1) and t<=element(periods,ccu_e_ctc(ccu,'4','6')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= ColdTransCost(ccu,'4','6')*(Uc(ccu,'6',t) - Sum[ccu_ct0 | ccu_ct0 >= First(Periods)
                                        and ccu_ct0 <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'5',ccu_ct0) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_ct0)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint InitCCUWarmA4Trans6CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t) | t>element(Periods, ccu_s_4watc6(ccu)+1) and t<=element(periods,ccu_e_watc(ccu,'4','6')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= WarmATransCost(ccu,'4','6')*(Uc(ccu,'6',t) - Sum[ccu_wat0 | ccu_wat0 >= First(Periods)
                                        and ccu_wat0 <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'5',ccu_wat0) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_wat0)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint InitCCUWarmB4Trans6CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t) | t>element(Periods, ccu_s_4wbtc6(ccu)+1) and t<=element(periods,ccu_e_wbtc(ccu,'4','6')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= WarmBTransCost(ccu,'4','6')*(Uc(ccu,'6',t) - Sum[ccu_wbt0 | ccu_wbt0 >= First(Periods)
                                        and ccu_wbt0 <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'5',ccu_wbt0) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_wbt0)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint CCUCold4Trans6CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t)| t>element(Periods,ccu_e_ctc(ccu,'4','6')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= ColdTransCost(ccu,'4','6')*(Uc(ccu,'6',t) - Sum[ccu_ct | ccu_ct >= t - TransTimeToCold(ccu,'4','6')
                                        and ccu_ct <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'5',ccu_ct) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_ct)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint CCUWarmA4Trans6CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t)| t>element(Periods,ccu_e_watc(ccu,'4','6')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= WarmATransCost(ccu,'4','6')*(Uc(ccu,'6',t) - Sum[ccu_wat | ccu_wat >= t - TransTimeToWarmA(ccu,'4','6')
                                        and ccu_wat <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'5',ccu_wat) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_wat)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint CCUWarmB4Trans6CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t)| t>element(Periods,ccu_e_wbtc(ccu,'4','6')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= WarmBTransCost(ccu,'4','6')*(Uc(ccu,'6',t) - Sum[ccu_wbt | ccu_wbt >= t - TransTimeToWarmB(ccu,'4','6')
                                        and ccu_wbt <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'5',ccu_wbt) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_wbt)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint InitCCUCold5Trans6CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t) | t>element(Periods, ccu_s_5ctc6(ccu)+1) and t<=element(periods,ccu_e_ctc(ccu,'5','6')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= ColdTransCost(ccu,'5','6')*(Uc(ccu,'6',t) - Sum[ccu_ct0 | ccu_ct0 >= First(Periods)
                                        and ccu_ct0 <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'4',ccu_ct0) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_ct0)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint InitCCUWarmA5Trans6CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t) | t>element(Periods, ccu_s_5watc6(ccu)+1) and t<=element(periods,ccu_e_watc(ccu,'5','6')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= WarmATransCost(ccu,'5','6')*(Uc(ccu,'6',t) - Sum[ccu_wat0 | ccu_wat0 >= First(Periods)
                                        and ccu_wat0 <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'4',ccu_wat0) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_wat0)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint InitCCUWarmB5Trans6CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t) | t>element(Periods, ccu_s_5wbtc6(ccu)+1) and t<=element(periods,ccu_e_wbtc(ccu,'5','6')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= WarmBTransCost(ccu,'5','6')*(Uc(ccu,'6',t) - Sum[ccu_wbt0 | ccu_wbt0 >= First(Periods)
                                        and ccu_wbt0 <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'4',ccu_wbt0) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_wbt0)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint CCUCold5Trans6CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t)| t>element(Periods,ccu_e_ctc(ccu,'5','6')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= ColdTransCost(ccu,'5','6')*(Uc(ccu,'6',t) - Sum[ccu_ct | ccu_ct >= t - TransTimeToCold(ccu,'5','6')
                                        and ccu_ct <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'4',ccu_ct) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_ct)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint CCUWarmA5Trans6CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t)| t>element(Periods,ccu_e_watc(ccu,'5','6')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= WarmATransCost(ccu,'5','6')*(Uc(ccu,'6',t) - Sum[ccu_wat | ccu_wat >= t - TransTimeToWarmA(ccu,'5','6')
                                        and ccu_wat <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'4',ccu_wat) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_wat)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint CCUWarmB5Trans6CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t)| t>element(Periods,ccu_e_wbtc(ccu,'5','6')+1);
                            Definition: {
                                ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >= WarmBTransCost(ccu,'5','6')*(Uc(ccu,'6',t) - Sum[ccu_wbt | ccu_wbt >= t - TransTimeToWarmB(ccu,'5','6')
                                        and ccu_wbt <= t - 1, Uc(ccu,'4',ccu_wbt) + Uc(ccu,'6',ccu_wbt)])
                            }
                        }
                        Constraint CCUCold3Trans6CostConstraint {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,t);
                            Definition: ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t) >=ColdTransCost(ccu,'3','6') * ( Uc(ccu,'3',t-1) + Uc(ccu,'6',t) - 1 );
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            Section ApplicationFunctions {
                DeclarationSection UnitFixedOutPutFunctions {
                    Constraint FixedUi {
                        IndexDomain: (i,t) in FixedScheduleSet | FixedOutPutPower(i,t) >= Pmin(i,t);
                        Definition: Ui(i,t) = 1;
                    }
                    Constraint FixedPower {
                        IndexDomain: (i,t) in FixedScheduleSet;
                        Definition: Pi(i,t) = FixedOutPutPower(i,t);
                    }
                    Constraint ModeFixedPowerConstraints {
                        IndexDomain: (ccu,m,t) in CCUnitModeFixPowerSet;
                        Definition: mP(ccu,m,t) = CCUnitModeFixPower(ccu,m,t);
                    }
                }
                DeclarationSection UnitFixedOnOffFunctions {
                    Constraint fixedOnOffConstraints {
                        IndexDomain: (ele,t)|(ele,t) in FixedOnOffSet and ele in ThermalUnitSet;
                        Definition: Ui(ele,t) = FixedOnOffList(ele,t);
                    }
                    Constraint ModeFixedOnOffConstraints {
                        IndexDomain: (ccu,m,t) in ModeFixedOnOffSet;
                        Definition: Uc(ccu,m,t) = ModeFixedOnOffList(ccu,m,t);
                    }
                }
                DeclarationSection UnitReserveFunctions {
                    Constraint UnitReserveConstraints {
                        IndexDomain: (i,t) in UnitReserveSet;
                        Definition: ( Pmax(i,t) - Pi(i,t) ) >= UnitReserveList(i,t);
                    }
                }
                DeclarationSection HydroEnergyFunctions {
                    Constraint HydroEnergyConstraints_Up {
                        IndexDomain: hdp;
                        Definition: {
                            sum[(i,t)|HydroPlantUnitList(hdp,i), Pi(i,t)]* PrdMin / 60
                            <=HydroEnergyLimit(hdp)
                        }
                    }
                    Constraint HydroEnergyConstraints_Down {
                        IndexDomain: (hdp);
                        Definition: {
                            sum[(i,t)|HydroPlantUnitList(hdp,i), Pi(i,t)]
                            * PrdMin / 60
                            >=
                            HydroEnergyLimitDown(hdp)
                        }
                    }
                }
                DeclarationSection RegionVoltageFunctions {
                    Constraint RegionVoltagePowerConstraints {
                        IndexDomain: (rvs,t);
                        Definition: sum[ i|RegionVoltageUnitList(rvs,i), Pi(i,t)] <= RegionVoltagePowerLimit(rvs,t);
                    }
                    Constraint RegionVoltagePowerConstraints_Down {
                        IndexDomain: (rvs,t);
                        Definition: sum[ i|RegionVoltageUnitList(rvs,i), Pi(i,t)] >= RegionVoltagePowerLimitDown(rvs,t);
                    }
                }
                DeclarationSection RegionReserveFunctions {
                    Constraint RegionReservePowerConstraints {
                        IndexDomain: (rrs,t);
                        Definition: sum[ i | RegionReserveUnitList(rrs,i), Pmax(i,t)*Ui(i,t)-Pi(i,t) ] >= RegionReservePowerLimit(rrs,t);
                    }
                    Constraint RegionReservePowerConstraints_Down {
                        IndexDomain: (rrs,t);
                        Definition: sum[ i | RegionReserveUnitList(rrs,i), Pi(i,t)-Pmin(i,t)*Ui(i,t) ] >= RegionReservePowerLimitDown(rrs,t);
                    }
                }
            }

                MathematicalProgram UnitCommitment {
                    Objective: TotalCost;
                    Direction: minimize;
                    Constraints: SCUCConstraintsSet;
                    Type: MIP;
                }
                Variable TotalCost {
                    Definition: {
                        sum[(i,t), Ci(i,t)+Si(i,t)]
                        
                        !!+ sum[(ccu,t) , mCost(ccu,t)  + ccuTCost(ccu,t) + ccu4ModeTcost(ccu,t)]
                        !!+ sum[(i,t), Ci(i,t)+Si(i,t)]
                        !!+CCUTotalRunningCost
                        !+sum[(tie,t) , tieCost(tie,t)]
                        
                        !+AbandonWindEnergyCost
                        !+AbandonWindPowerCost
                        
                        
                        !!+ Nop_Cost
                        
                        !VioTiePowerPF
                        !+sum[(tie,t)|tieline_fix_direction(tie,t)<0,-1*tieP(tie,t)*VioTiePowerPF]!!sell max
                        !+sum[(tie,t)|tieline_fix_direction(tie,t)>0,tieP(tie,t)*VioTiePowerPF]!buy minimum
                        
                        
                        +sum[(nfg,t),NFGLimitRelax_up(nfg,t)*NFGLimitRelaxPunishCoeff(nfg)]
                        
                        
                        !+sum[(nfg,t),NFGLimitRelax_down(nfg,t)*NFGLimitRelaxPunishCoeff(nfg)] !xuebike edit 20150422
                        
                        +sum[(i,t),PowerBiasRelax(i,t)*PowerBiasVio]
                    }
                }
                Parameter ccuTotalCost {
                    Definition: sum[(ccu,t) , mCost(ccu,t)  + ccuTCost(ccu,t)];
                }
                Parameter tunitTotalCost {
                    Definition: sum[(i,t), Ci(i,t)+Si(i,t)];
                }
                Parameter TieLineTotalCost {
                    Definition: sum[(tie,t) , tieCost(tie,t)];
                }

        Section InterfaceDef {
            Section InputInterface {
                DeclarationSection SharedPara {
                    StringParameter Path_in;
                    StringParameter Path_out;
                    StringParameter path_out_tmp;
                    StringParameter Data_check_path;
                    StringParameter GFG_path_in;
                    Parameter CostBlockNum {
                        Range: integer;
                    }
                    Parameter index_temp {
                        Range: {
                            {1..inf}
                        }
                    }
                    Parameter index_period {
                        Range: integer;
                    }
                    StringParameter UnitName_Input;
                    ElementParameter UnitSet_ele {
                        Range: EleSet;
                    }
                    Parameter PrdId_Input {
                        Range: integer;
                    }
                    ElementParameter Periods_ele {
                        Range: Periods;
                    }
                    StringParameter NFGName_Input;
                    ElementParameter NFGSet_ele {
                        Range: NormalFlowGateSet;
                    }
                    StringParameter GFGName_Input;
                    ElementParameter GFGSet_ele {
                        Range: GeneratedFlowGateSet;
                    }

                    ElementParameter HDPSet_ele {
                        Range: HydroPlantSet;

                    ElementParameter RVSet_ele {
                        Range: RegionVoltageSet;
                    }

                    ElementParameter RRSet_ele {
                        Range: RegionReserveSet;
                    }
                    StringParameter ResourceGroupName_Input;
                    ElementParameter ResourceGroupSet_ele {
                        Range: ResourceGroupSet;
                    }
                    StringParameter EnvironmentGroupName_Input;
                    ElementParameter EnvironmentGroupSet_ele {
                        Range: EnvironmentGroupSet;
                    }
                    ElementParameter CCUSet_ele {
                        Range: CCUnitSet;
                    }
                    ElementParameter ItsSet_ele {
                        Range: ItsSet;
                    }
                }
                Section Common_InitialState_Input {
                    DeclarationSection Comon_InitialState_Para {
                        Parameter Common_UnitInitNum {
                            Range: integer;
                        }
                        Parameter Common_InitialUi_Input {
                            Range: binary;
                        }
                        Parameter Common_InitialPi_Input;
                        Parameter Common_InitialXOni_Input {
                            Range: integer;
                        }
                        Parameter Common_InitialXOffi_Input {
                            Range: integer;
                        }
                    }
                    ExternalFunction Common_get_unitinit_num_ext {
                        Arguments: (path);
                        DllName: DllFileName;
                        ReturnType: integer;
                        BodyCall: Common_Get_UnitInit_Num(scalar : path);
                        StringParameter path {
                            Property: Input;
                        }
                    }
                    ExternalProcedure Common_get_unitinit_data_ext {
                        Arguments: (a);
                        DllName: DllFileName;
                        BodyCall: Common_Get_UnitInit_Data( scalar : a );
                        Parameter a {
                            Range: {
                                {1..inf}
                            }
                            Property: Input;
                        }
                    }
                    Procedure Common_InitialState_Init {
                        Body: {
                            Common_UnitInitNum := Common_get_unitinit_num_ext(Path_in);
                            
                            index_temp := 1;
                            while(index_temp <= Common_UnitInitNum) do
                                    Common_get_unitinit_data_ext(index_temp);
                            
                                    UnitSet_ele := StringToElement (EleSet , UnitName_Input , create : 0);
                            
                                    ele_InitStatus(UnitSet_ele) := Common_InitialUi_Input;
                                    ele_InitPower(UnitSet_ele) := Common_InitialPi_Input;
                                    ele_InitOnTime(UnitSet_ele) := Common_InitialXOni_Input;
                                    ele_InitOffTime(UnitSet_ele) := Common_InitialXOffi_Input;
                            
                                    index_temp += 1;
                            endwhile;
                        }
                    }
                }

                        ExternalFunction get_tunit_num_ext {
                            Arguments: (path);

                                Property: Input;
                            }
                        }
                        ExternalProcedure get_tunit_data_ext {
                            Arguments: (a);
                            DllName: DllFileName;
                            BodyCall: Get_TUnit_Data(scalar : a );
                            Parameter a {
                                Range: {
                                    {1..inf}
                                }
                                Property: Input;
                            }
                        }
                        Procedure TUnitGeneral_Init {
                            Body: {
                                TUnitNum := get_tunit_num_ext(Path_in) ;
                                
                                index_temp := 1 ;
                                while(index_temp <= TUnitNum) do
                                        get_tunit_data_ext(index_temp);
                                
                                        t_UnId_ele := StringToElement (ThermalUnitSet , t_UnId_Input , create : 0);
                                
                                        FuelType(t_UnId_ele) := t_Type_tmp;
                                
                                        !Pmax(t_UnId_ele , t) := t_Pmax_tmp;
                                        !Pmin(t_UnId_ele , t) := t_Pmin_tmp;
                                
                                        Reg_Pmax(t_UnId_ele) := t_Pmax_tmp;
                                        Reg_Pmin(t_UnId_ele) := t_Pmin_tmp;
                                
                                        Capacity(t_UnId_ele) := t_Cap_tmp;
                                
                                        MinOnTime(t_UnId_ele) := t_MinOn_tmp ;
                                        MinOffTime(t_UnId_ele) := t_MinOff_tmp ;
                                        MinOnTimeTemp(t_UnId_ele) := t_MinOn_tmp ;
                                        MinOffTimeTemp(t_UnId_ele) := t_MinOff_tmp ;
                                
                                        RampUp(t_UnId_ele) := t_RU_tmp;
                                        RampDown(t_UnId_ele) := t_RD_tmp;
                                
                                        ColdStartCost(t_UnId_ele) := t_ColdCost_tmp;
                                        WarmStartCost(t_UnId_ele) := t_WarmCost_tmp;
                                        HotStartCost(t_UnId_ele) := t_HotCost_tmp;
                                
                                        CO2(t_UnId_ele) := t_CO2_tmp;
                                        SO2(t_UnId_ele) := t_SO2_tmp;
                                        NOX(t_UnId_ele) := t_NOX_tmp;
                                        OEm(t_UnId_ele) := t_OEm_tmp;
                                        EnvironmentMinUpTime(t_UnId_ele) :=  t_EcoMinOnTime_tmp;
                                        EnvironmentMinDownTime(t_UnId_ele) := t_EcoMinOffTime_tmp;
                                        index_temp += 1;
                                endwhile;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    Section TUnitCostInput {
                        DeclarationSection UnitCostPara {
                            Parameter UnitCostNum {
                                Range: integer;
                            }
                            Parameter CostId_Input {
                                Range: free;
                            }
                            ElementParameter CostBlockSet_ele {
                                Range: CostBlockSet;
                            }
                            Parameter UnitCost_out1_Input;
                            Parameter UnitCost_out2_Input;
                            Parameter UnitCost_price_Input;
                            Parameter UnitCost_netcost_Input;
                            Parameter UnitCost_inccost_Input;
                        }
                        ExternalFunction get_unitcost_num_ext {
                            Arguments: (path);
                            DllName: DllFileName;
                            ReturnType: integer;
                            BodyCall: Get_UnitCost_Num(scalar : path);
                            StringParameter path {
                                Property: Input;
                            }
                        }
                        ExternalProcedure get_unitcost_data_ext {
                            Arguments: (a);
                            DllName: DllFileName;
                            BodyCall: Get_UnitCost_Data(scalar : a );
                            Parameter a {
                                Range: {
                                    {1..inf}
                                }
                                Property: Input;
                            }
                        }
                        Procedure UnitCost_Init {
                            Body: {
                                UnitCostNum := get_unitcost_num_ext(Path_in);
                                
                                index_temp := 1;
                                while(index_temp <= UnitCostNum) do
                                        get_unitcost_data_ext(index_temp);
                                
                                        UnitSet_ele := StringToElement (ThermalUnitSet , UnitName_Input , create : 0);
                                        CostBlockSet_ele := Element (CostBlockSet , CostId_Input);
                                        Periods_ele := Element (Periods , PrdId_Input + 1);
                                
                                        if (IsMultiCost = 1) then
                                                UnitBaseCost( UnitSet_ele , CostBlockSet_ele , Periods_ele) := UnitCost_netcost_Input;
                                                !UnitBaseCost( UnitSet_ele , CostBlockSet_ele , Periods_ele) := UnitCost_netcost_Input*CCAHeatCurveMove;
                                                UnitIncCost( UnitSet_ele , CostBlockSet_ele , Periods_ele) := UnitCost_inccost_Input;
                                                CostBlockStart( UnitSet_ele , CostBlockSet_ele , Periods_ele) := UnitCost_out1_Input;
                                                CostBlockEnd( UnitSet_ele , CostBlockSet_ele , Periods_ele) := UnitCost_out2_Input;
                                
                                        else
                                                Reg_UnitBaseCost( UnitSet_ele , CostBlockSet_ele ) := UnitCost_netcost_Input;
                                                !Reg_UnitBaseCost( UnitSet_ele , CostBlockSet_ele ) := UnitCost_netcost_Input*CCAHeatCurveMove;
                                                Reg_UnitIncCost( UnitSet_ele , CostBlockSet_ele ) := UnitCost_inccost_Input;
                                                Reg_CostBlockStart( UnitSet_ele , CostBlockSet_ele ) := UnitCost_out1_Input;
                                                Reg_CostBlockEnd( UnitSet_ele , CostBlockSet_ele ) := UnitCost_out2_Input;
                                
                                                UnitBaseCost( UnitSet_ele , CostBlockSet_ele , t) := Reg_UnitBaseCost( UnitSet_ele , CostBlockSet_ele );
                                                UnitIncCost( UnitSet_ele , CostBlockSet_ele , t) := Reg_UnitIncCost( UnitSet_ele , CostBlockSet_ele );
                                                CostBlockStart( UnitSet_ele , CostBlockSet_ele , t) := Reg_CostBlockStart( UnitSet_ele , CostBlockSet_ele );
                                                CostBlockEnd( UnitSet_ele , CostBlockSet_ele , t) := Reg_CostBlockEnd( UnitSet_ele , CostBlockSet_ele );
                                
                                        endif;
                                
                                        index_temp += 1;
                                endwhile;
                                
                                /*
                                for(i,t) do
                                
                                        if( CostBlockStart(i,'10',t) > CostBlockEnd(i,'10',t) ) then
                                
                                                CostBlockEnd(i,'10',t) := Pmax(i,t) ;
                                
                                        endif ;
                                
                                endfor ;
                                */
                            }
                        }
                    }

                    Section ThermalOSPmaxPminInput {
                        DeclarationSection ThermalOSPmaxPminPara {

                        ExternalFunction ThermalOS_get_unit_power_limit_temp_num_ext {
                            Arguments: (path);
                            DllName: DllFileName;
                            ReturnType: integer;
                            BodyCall: ThermalOS_Get_UnitPowerLimitTemp_Num(scalar : path);
                            StringParameter path {
                                Property: Input;

                        ExternalProcedure ThermalOS_get_unit_power_limit_temp_data_ext {
                            Arguments: (a);
                            DllName: DllFileName;
                            BodyCall: ThermalOS_Get_UnitPowerLimitTemp_Data(scalar : a);
                            Parameter a {
                                Range: {
                                    {1..inf}
                                }
                                Property: Input;
                            }
                        }
                        Procedure ThermalOS_UnitPowerLimitTemp_Init {
                            Body: {
                                !! comments by xuebike
                                !! This procedure deals with which thermal units have power limit.
                                !! and initialize the  parameter ThermalOS_IsExist_Pmax_Temp,and
                                !! ThermalOS_Pmax_Temp ,ThermalOS_Pmin_Temp.
                                
                                ThermalOS_UnitPowerLimitTempNum := ThermalOS_get_unit_power_limit_temp_num_ext( Path_in ) ;
                                
                                index_temp := 1;
                                while(index_temp <= ThermalOS_UnitPowerLimitTempNum) do
                                
                                        !!comments by xuebike
                                        !!According the index_temp,call the external function ThermalOS_get_unit_power_limit_temp_data_ext
                                        !!get the parameters "UnitName_Input,PrdId_Input,ThermalOS_limit_temp_minout_tmp
                                        !!and ThermalOS_limit_temp_minout_tmp" corresponding the index_temp.
                                        ThermalOS_get_unit_power_limit_temp_data_ext(index_temp);
                                
                                        !!According the UnitName_Input,get the corresponding UnitSet_ele.
                                        UnitSet_ele := StringToElement (ThermalUnitSet , UnitName_Input , create : 0);
                                
                                        Periods_ele := Element (Periods , PrdId_Input + 1);
                                
                                
                                        ThermalOS_IsExist_Pmax_Temp(UnitSet_ele , Periods_ele) := 1 ;
                                
                                        ThermalOS_Pmax_Temp(UnitSet_ele , Periods_ele) := ThermalOS_limit_temp_maxout_tmp;
                                        ThermalOS_Pmin_Temp(UnitSet_ele , Periods_ele) := ThermalOS_limit_temp_minout_tmp;
                                
                                
                                        index_temp += 1;
                                endwhile;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }

                    Procedure NFG_Init {
                        Body: {
                            nfg_input_ext(Path_in);
                            
                            index_period := 1;
                            while(index_period <= NT) do
                            
                                    NFGLimitNum := get_nfglimit_num_ext(Path_in , index_period);
                                    index_temp := 1;
                                    while(index_temp <= NFGLimitNum) do
                            
                                            get_nfglimit_data_ext(index_temp);
                            
                                            NFGSet_ele := StringToElement(NormalFlowGateSet , NFGName_Input , create : 0);
                                            Periods_ele := Element (Periods , index_period + 1);
                                            NFGLimit( NFGSet_ele , Periods_ele) := NFGLimit_Input;
                                            NFGLoad( NFGSet_ele , Periods_ele) := NFGLoad_Input;
                            
                                            index_temp += 1;
                                    endwhile;
                            
                                    index_period += 1;
                            endwhile;
                            
                            
                            
                            index_period := 1;
                            while(index_period <= NT) do
                            
                                    NFGSensNum := get_nfgsens_num_ext(Path_in , index_period);
                                    index_temp := 1;
                            
                                    while (index_temp <= NFGSensNum) do
                            
                                            get_nfgsens_data_ext(index_temp);
                            
                                            UnitSet_ele := StringToElement (EleSet , UnitName_Input , create : 0);
                                            NFGSet_ele := StringToElement(NormalFlowGateSet , NFGName_Input , create : 0);
                                            Periods_ele := Element (Periods , index_period + 1);
                            
                                            NFGSens( UnitSet_ele , NFGSet_ele , Periods_ele ) := NFGSens_Input;
                            
                                            index_temp += 1;
                                    endwhile;
                            
                                    index_period += 1;
                            endwhile;
                        }
                    }

                            gfg_input_ext(GFG_path_in );

                            !while(index_period <= 2) do
                            while(index_period <= NT) do
                            
                                    GFGSensNum := get_gfgsens_num_ext(GFG_path_in , index_period);
                            
                                    index_temp := 1;
                                    while(index_temp <= GFGSensNum) do

                            NFG_Limit_Change ;
                            Calculate_ccu_gfg_sens ;
                        }

                        ExternalProcedure get_ccunit_cost_data_ext {
                            Arguments: (a);
                            DllName: DllFileName;
                            BodyCall: Get_CCUnitCost_Data(scalar : a );
                            Parameter a {
                                Range: {
                                    {1..inf}
                                }
                                Property: Input;
                            }
                        }
                        Procedure CCUnitCost_Init {
                            Body: {
                                CCUnitCostNum := get_ccunit_cost_num_ext(Path_in) ;
                                
                                index_temp := 1 ;
                                while(index_temp <= CCUnitCostNum) do
                                        get_ccunit_cost_data_ext(index_temp);
                                
                                        cc_UnId_ele := StringToElement (CCUnitSet , cc_UnId_Input , create : 0);
                                        cc_ModeId_ele := Element(ModeSet , cc_ModeId_Input + 1 ) ;
                                        cc_CostId_ele := Element (CostBlockSet , cc_CostId_Input);
                                        cc_PrdId_ele := Element (Periods , cc_PrdId_Input + 1);
                                
                                
                                        if (IsMultiCost = 1) then
                                
                                                ccuCostBlockStart(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele , cc_PrdId_ele ) := cc_out1_tmp ;
                                                ccuCostBlockEnd(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele , cc_PrdId_ele ) := cc_out2_tmp ;
                                                ccuBaseCost(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele , cc_PrdId_ele ) := cc_netcost_tmp*HeatCurveMove ;
                                                ccuIncCost(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele , cc_PrdId_ele ) := cc_inccost_tmp ;
                                
                                
                                        else
                                
                                                Reg_ccuCostBlockStart(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele) := cc_out1_tmp ;
                                                Reg_ccuCostBlockEnd(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele) := cc_out2_tmp ;
                                                Reg_ccuBaseCost(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele) := cc_netcost_tmp*HeatCurveMove ;
                                                Reg_ccuIncCost(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele) := cc_inccost_tmp ;
                                
                                
                                                ccuCostBlockStart(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele , t )
                                                                := cc_out1_tmp ;
                                                ccuCostBlockEnd(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele , t)
                                                                := cc_out2_tmp ;
                                                ccuBaseCost(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele , t)
                                                                := cc_netcost_tmp*HeatCurveMove ;
                                                ccuIncCost(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele , t)
                                                                := cc_inccost_tmp ;
                                
                                
                                        endif ;
                                
                                /*
                                        ccuCostBlockStart(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele) := cc_out1_tmp ;
                                        ccuCostBlockEnd(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele) := cc_out2_tmp ;
                                        ccuBaseCost(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele) := cc_netcost_tmp ;
                                        ccuIncCost(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele) := cc_inccost_tmp ;
                                */
                                
                                        index_temp += 1;
                                endwhile;
                            }
                        }
                    }

                        Procedure CCUnitInit_Init {
                            Body: {
                                !! Read From E-file
                                /*
                                CCUnitInitNum := get_ccunit_init_num_ext(Path_in) ;
                                
                                index_temp := 1 ;
                                while(index_temp <= CCUnitInitNum) do
                                        get_ccunit_init_data_ext(index_temp);

                                        cc_ModeId_ele := Element(ModeSet , cc_ModeId_Input + 1 ) ;
                                
                                        InitMode( cc_UnId_ele ) := cc_ModeId_ele;
                                        InitTime( cc_UnId_ele ) := cc_init_time_tmp ;
                                        InitP( cc_UnId_ele ) := cc_init_power_tmp ;
                                
                                
                                        index_temp += 1;
                                endwhile;
                                */
                                
                                !! Calulate by ele_element  modify by G.J. 2010-1-8;
                                CCU_ele_initialState_Init;
                                
                                CCUModeInitStatusSet ;
                            }
                        }
                        Procedure CCU_ele_initialState_Init {
                            Body: {
                                for (ccu)  do
                                
                                
                                        !! ********  Judge Mode 0 **********
                                        AS_IsMode0 := 1;
                                        for (gst| CCUMemberList(ccu, gst) =1) do
                                
                                                if(ele_InitStatus(gst) =1 ) then
                                                        AS_IsMode0 := 0;
                                                        break;
                                                endif;
                                
                                        endfor;
                                
                                        if(AS_IsMode0 ) then
                                                InitMode( ccu ) := first(ModeSet);
                                                InitTime( ccu ) :=  min ( gst|CCUMemberList(ccu, gst)=1, ele_InitOffTime( gst)   );
                                                InitP(ccu) := 0;
                                                break;
                                        endif;
                                
                                
                                
                                        !! ********  Judge Mode 1-Nmode(6)
                                
                                        for ( m | val(m)>0 and val(m)<=NMode(ccu)   )do
                                
                                                AS_IsCurrentMode_GT := 0 ;
                                                AS_IsCurrentMode_ST := 0 ;
                                                AS_ModeTime := 8760000;
                                                AS_ModePower :=0;
                                
                                                !!  Search  GT  units
                                                for(gt|ModeGTList(ccu,m,gt)=1 ) do
                                
                                                        if( ele_InitStatus(gt) = 1)  then
                                
                                                                AS_ModePower := AS_ModePower + ele_InitPower(gt);
                                                                if( ele_InitOnTime(gt) < AS_ModeTime) then  AS_ModeTime :=ele_InitOnTime(gt); endif;
                                                                As_IsCurrentMode_GT := 1 ;
                                                        else
                                                                As_IsCurrentMode_GT := 0 ;
                                                                break;
                                                        endif;
                                
                                
                                                endfor;
                                
                                
                                                !!  Search  ST  units
                                                if(max(st, ModeSTList(ccu,m,st))=0) then AS_IsCurrentMode_ST :=1 ;  endif;
                                
                                                for(st|ModeSTList(ccu,m,st)=1 ) do
                                
                                                        if( ele_InitStatus(st) = 1)  then
                                                                AS_ModePower := AS_ModePower + ele_InitPower(st);
                                                                if( ele_InitOnTime(st) < AS_ModeTime) then  AS_ModeTime :=ele_InitOnTime(st); endif;
                                                                As_IsCurrentMode_ST := 1 ;
                                                        else
                                                                As_IsCurrentMode_ST := 0 ;
                                                                break;
                                                        endif;
                                
                                                 endfor;
                                
                                
                                                !! Dispose Mode m : 1-5
                                                if( AS_IsCurrentMode_GT and AS_IsCurrentMode_ST) then
                                
                                                        InitMode( ccu ) := m;
                                                        InitTime( ccu ) := AS_ModeTime;
                                                        InitP(ccu) := AS_ModePower;
                                
                                
                                                        !!break;
                                
                                                endif;
                                
                                        endfor;  !!m
                                
                                
                                
                                endfor;  !! ccu
                            }
                        }
                        DeclarationSection CCU_ele_Init_praa {
                            Parameter AS_ModePower;
                            Parameter AS_ModeOffTime;
                            Parameter AS_ModeTime;
                            Parameter AS_IsCurrentMode_GT {
                                Range: binary;
                            }
                            Parameter AS_IsCurrentMode_ST {
                                Range: binary;
                            }
                            Parameter AS_IsMode0 {
                                Range: binary;
                            }
                        }

                        Procedure CCUnitHeat_Init {
                            Body: {
                                CCUnitHeatNum := get_ccunit_heat_num_ext(Path_in) ;
                                
                                index_temp := 1 ;
                                while(index_temp <= CCUnitHeatNum) do
                                        get_ccunit_heat_data_ext(index_temp);

                                        cc_ModeId_ele := Element(ModeSet , cc_ModeId_Input + 1 ) ;
                                        cc_HeatId_ele := Element (CostBlockSet , cc_HeatId_Input);
                                        cc_PrdId_ele := Element (Periods , cc_PrdId_Input + 1);
                                
                                
                                        if (IsMultiCost = 1) then
                                
                                                ccuHeatBlockStart(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_HeatId_ele , cc_PrdId_ele ) := cc_heat_out1_tmp ;
                                                ccuHeatBlockEnd(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_HeatId_ele , cc_PrdId_ele ) := cc_heat_out2_tmp ;
                                                ccuBaseHeat(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_HeatId_ele , cc_PrdId_ele ) := cc_netheat_tmp*HeatCurveMove ;
                                                ccuIncHeat(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_HeatId_ele , cc_PrdId_ele ) := cc_incheat_tmp ;
                                                !ccuBaseHeat(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_HeatId_ele , cc_PrdId_ele ) := cc_heat_out1_tmp*cc_incheat_tmp;
                                
                                        else
                                
                                                Reg_ccuHeatBlockStart(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_HeatId_ele) := cc_heat_out1_tmp ;
                                                Reg_ccuHeatBlockEnd(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_HeatId_ele) := cc_heat_out2_tmp ;
                                                Reg_ccuBaseHeat(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_HeatId_ele) := cc_netheat_tmp*HeatCurveMove ;
                                                Reg_ccuIncHeat(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_HeatId_ele) := cc_incheat_tmp ;
                                                !Reg_ccuBaseHeat(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_HeatId_ele) := cc_heat_out1_tmp*cc_incheat_tmp;
                                
                                                ccuHeatBlockStart(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_HeatId_ele , t ) := cc_heat_out1_tmp ;
                                                ccuHeatBlockEnd(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_HeatId_ele , t)
                                                                := cc_heat_out2_tmp ;
                                                ccuBaseHeat(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_HeatId_ele , t) := cc_netheat_tmp*HeatCurveMove;
                                                ccuIncHeat(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_HeatId_ele , t)
                                                                := cc_incheat_tmp ;
                                
                                
                                        endif ;
                                
                                /*
                                        ccuCostBlockStart(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele) := cc_out1_tmp ;
                                        ccuCostBlockEnd(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele) := cc_out2_tmp ;
                                        ccuBaseCost(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele) := cc_netcost_tmp ;
                                        ccuIncCost(cc_UnId_ele , cc_ModeId_ele , cc_CostId_ele) := cc_inccost_tmp ;
                                */
                                
                                        index_temp += 1;
                                endwhile;
                            }
                        }
                    }

                            Body: {
                                CCUGasHeatRateNum := get_ccu_gas_heat_rate_num_ext(Path_in);
                                
                                index_temp := 1;
                                while(index_temp <= CCUGasHeatRateNum) do
                                
                                        get_ccu_tunit_gas_heat_rate_data_ext(index_temp);

                                        Periods_ele := Element (Periods , PrdId_Input + 1);
                                
                                        CCUHeatRate(cc_UnId_ele  , Periods_ele) := CCUHeatRateTmp;
                                
                                
                                        index_temp += 1;
                                endwhile;
                            }
                        }
                    }
