                Section PostCalcuate {
                    DeclarationSection OutPutPara {
                        Parameter tt {
                            IndexDomain: (i);
                            Definition: sum(t,average_cost(i,t))/96;
                        }
                        Parameter average_cost {
                            IndexDomain: (i,t);
                            Definition: Ci(i,t)/ (pi(i,t)+0.0000000001) /prdmin*60;
                        }
                        Parameter AS_LoadBalance_out {
                            IndexDomain: (t);
                            Definition: AS_TotalGeneration_out(t) - Load(t);
                        }
                        Parameter AS_TotalGeneration_out {
                            IndexDomain: (t);
                            Definition: sum(ele,p(ele,t));
                        }
                        Parameter mGTCapacity {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m);
                            Definition: sum[gt |ModeGTList(ccu,m,gt)=1,  GSTPmax(gt)];
                        }
                        Parameter mSTCapacity {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m);
                            Definition: sum[st |ModeSTList(ccu,m,st)=1,  GSTPmax(st)];
                        }
                        Parameter CCU_st_total_p {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu);
                        }
                        Parameter CCU_ct_total_p {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu);
                        }
                        Parameter CCU_leftGT_total_p {
                            IndexDomain: (ccu,m,t);
                        }
                        Parameter Tie_total_p {
                            IndexDomain: (t);
                            Definition: sum (tie, tieP(tie,t));
                        }
                        Parameter Its_total_p {
                            IndexDomain: (its,t);
                            Definition: sum (tie|ItsTielineList(its,tie), tieP(tie,t));
                        }
                        Parameter Its_total_rate {
                            IndexDomain: (its,t);
                            Definition: sum (tie|ItsTielineList(its,tie), TieDecomRate(tie,t)*TieIsRun(tie,t));
                        }
                    }
                    Procedure DecomCCUResult {
                        Body: {
                            !!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!
                            !!
                            !!      PurPose : Decompose The CCU Mode optimal result into individed unit power output.
                            !!
                            !!
                            !!      Create By:  GengJian  2009-10-30
                            !!
                            !!      Last Edit: 2009-11-21
                            !!
                            !!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!
                            
                               P(gst,t) := 0.0;
                            
                               CCU_leftGT_total_p(ccu,m,t) := mp(ccu,m,t);
                            
                            
                            for (ccu,m, t)| Uc(ccu, m,t)=1 and m>'0' do
                            
                            
                               !! Decompose By Capacity Scale
                               /* for( st ) | ModeSTList(ccu,m,st)=1 do
                                    P(st,t) := mP(ccu,m,t) * GSTPmax(st)/ (mGTCapacity(ccu,m) + mSTCapacity(ccu,m)+ 0.000001);
                                endfor;
                            
                            
                                for( gt ) | ModeGTList(ccu,m,gt)=1 do
                                    P(gt,t) :=  mP(ccu,m,t) * GSTPmax(gt)/ (mGTCapacity(ccu,m) + mSTCapacity(ccu,m)+ 0.000001);
                                endfor;
                                */
                            
                            
                            
                                !! Decompose By 1/2 ST VS GT Sacle and  Decompose GT by Capacity Scale
                                for( st ) | ModeSTList(ccu,m,st)=1 do
                                    P(st,t) := mP(ccu,m,t) * 1/3;
                                    CCU_leftGT_total_p(ccu,m,t) :=  mP(ccu,m,t) - P(st,t) ;
                            
                                endfor;
                            
                            
                                for( gt ) | ModeGTList(ccu,m,gt)=1 do
                                    P(gt,t) :=  CCU_leftGT_total_p(ccu,m,t) * GSTPmax(gt)/ (mGTCapacity(ccu,m)+ 0.000001);
                                endfor;
                            
                            
                            endfor;
                        }
                    }
                    Procedure DecomTieRusult {
                        Body: {
                            !!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!
                            !!
                            !!      PurPose : Decompose The ITS -tie result into individed real run tie output.
                            !!
                            !!
                            !!      Warn:   If  TieIsRun or TieDecomRate is 0, the Tieline injection is serious error for SCS,
                            !!              SO, the two parameters are initialed 1.0 by default;
                            !!      Create By:  GengJian  2009-10-30
                            !!
                            !!      Last Edit: 2009-11-21
                            !!
                            !!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!
                            
                            
                            
                               P(tie,t) := 0.0;
                            
                            
                              P(tie,t) := tiep(tie,t);
                            
                            
                            /*
                               for(its,t)  do
                            
                                    for (tie) | ItsTielineList(its,tie) do
                            
                            
                                    P(tie,t) := Its_total_p(its,t) * TieIsRun(tie,t)* TieDecomRate(tie,t)  / (Its_total_Rate(Its,t)+0.0000001);
                            
                            
                                    endfor;
                            
                               endfor;
                            */
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            /*
                               for (tie,t) | tie = '1623000020' or tie = '1623000021' do
                            
                                 P(tie,t) := Tie_total_p(t)/2 ;
                            
                               endfor;
                            */
                        }
                    }
                    Procedure DecomTunitResult {
                        Body: {
                            !!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!
                            !!
                            !!      PurPose :Set Tunit Power to out parameters P.
                            !!
                            !!
                            !!      Create By:  GengJian  2009-10-30
                            !!
                            !!      Last Edit: 2009-11-21
                            !!
                            !!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!
                            
                               P(i,t) := 0.0;
                            
                               P(i,t) := Pi(i,t);
                        }
                    }
                    Procedure CalculatePrice {
                        Body: {
                            for(i,t) | Ui(i,t)  do
                            
                                    for(l) do
                                            if(  Pi(i,t)>=CostBlockStart(i,l,t) and Pi(i,t)<=CostBlockEnd(i,l,t)   )  then
                            
                                                    Price(i,t) := UnitIncCost(i,l,t) ;
                                                    break ;
                            
                                            endif ;
                            
                                    endfor ;
                            
                            endfor ;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        Section Static {
            Section PreCheckProcess {
                DeclarationSection DebugData {
                    Parameter availabe_power {
                        IndexDomain: t;
                        Definition: sum(i, pmax(i,t)) -sum( i |t<=element( Periods,( 1+ DTi(i) ) ), pmax(i,t) );
                    }
                    Parameter init_force_power_check {
                        Definition: {
                            Load('period-1')
                            -
                            sum
                            [
                            i | InitOnTime(i) < MinOnTime(i) and InitStatus(i)=1  ,
                            Pmin(i,'period-1')
                            ]
                        }
                    }
                    Parameter block_increse_check {
                        IndexDomain: (i,l,t);
                        Definition: costblockend(i,l,t)-costblockstart(i,l,t);
                    }
                    Parameter cost_min_check {
                        IndexDomain: (i,t);
                        Definition: pmin(i,t)-costblockstart(i,first(costblockset),t) + 0.0001;
                    }
                    Parameter cost_max_check {
                        IndexDomain: (i,t);
                        Definition: costblockend(i,last(costblockset),t)-pmax(i,t)+0.000001;
                    }
                    Parameter pre_load_balance {
                        IndexDomain: (t);
                        Definition: sum(i, pmax(i,t)) + sum(its, ItsPmax(its,t)) -Load(t);
                    }
                    Parameter cost_block {
                        IndexDomain: (i,l,t);
                        Definition: UnitIncCost(i,l,t)*pli(i,l,t);
                    }
                    Parameter fix_power_check {
                        IndexDomain: (i,t)in FixedScheduleSet;
                        Definition: FixedOutPutPower(i,t) - Pmin(i,t);
                    }
                    Parameter fix_power_max_check {
                        IndexDomain: (i,t)in FixedScheduleSet;
                        Definition: Pmax(i,t) - FixedOutPutPower(i,t);
                    }
                }
            }
            Section ResultStatics {
                DeclarationSection GeneralStaticPrameters {
                    Parameter AvaliableCapcity {
                        IndexDomain: (t);
                        Definition: {
                            sum[i,Ui(i,t)*Pmax(i,t)]
                            +
                            !sum[ccu , Uccu(ccu,t) * ccuPmax(ccu)]
                            sum[(ccu,m) , Uc(ccu,m,t)*mPmax(ccu,m,t)]
                        }
                    }
                    Parameter SupplyPower {
                        IndexDomain: (t);
                        Definition: {
                            sum[i,Pi(i,t)]
                            +
                            sum[(ccu,m) , mP(ccu,m,t)]
                        }
                    }
                    Parameter TieLinePower {
                        IndexDomain: (t);
                        Definition: sum[tie , tieline_fix_direction(tie,t)*tieP(tie,t)];
                    }
                    Parameter DeltaLoad {
                        IndexDomain: (t);
                        Definition: {
                            sum[i, Pi(i,t)]
                            +
                            sum[(ccu,m) , mP(ccu,m,t) ]
                            +
                            sum[tie , tieP(tie,t) ]
                            -
                            Load(t)
                        }
                    }
                    Parameter DeltaReserv {
                        IndexDomain: (t);
                        Definition: Rsv(t)-Reserve_Up(t);
                    }
                    Parameter Price {
                        IndexDomain: (i,t);
                    }
                    Parameter P {
                        IndexDomain: (ele,t);
                    }
                }
                DeclarationSection UnitGroup_Infomation {
                    Parameter unit_energy {
                        IndexDomain: (i);
                        Definition: sum[t,Pi(i,t) ]* PrdMin / 60;
                    }
                    Parameter group_energy {
                        IndexDomain: (hdp);
                        Definition: {
                            sum[(i,t)|HydroPlantUnitList(hdp,i), Pi(i,t)]
                            * PrdMin / 60
                        }
                    }
                    Parameter group_power {
                        IndexDomain: (rvs,t);
                        Definition: sum[ i|RegionVoltageUnitList(rvs,i), Pi(i,t)];
                    }
                    Parameter group_reserve {
                        IndexDomain: (rrs,t);
                        Definition: sum[ i | RegionReserveUnitList(rrs,i), Pmax(i,t)*Ui(i,t)-Pi(i,t) ];
                    }
                    Parameter group_reserve_down {
                        IndexDomain: (rrs,t);
                        Definition: sum[ i | RegionReserveUnitList(rrs,i), Pi(i,t)-Pmin(i,t)*Ui(i,t) ];
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

        DeclarationSection WindSunPowerCons {
            Parameter ExpectedWindPower {
                IndexDomain: (t);
            }
            Parameter SingleWindPlantPowerForecast {
                IndexDomain: (wd,t);
            }
            Constraint SingleWindPlantPowerCon {
                IndexDomain: (wd,t);
                Definition: Pi(wd,t)<=SingleWindPlantPowerForecast(wd,t);
            }
            Parameter SingleSunPlantPowerForecast {
                IndexDomain: (se,t);
            }
            Constraint SingleSunPlantPowerCon {
                IndexDomain: (se,t);
                Definition: Pi(se,t)<=SingleSunPlantPowerForecast(se,t);
            }

        DeclarationSection StatVariableDef {
            Variable EmissionNOx {
                Definition: (sum[(tu,t)|t>element(Periods,1),Pi(tu,t)]+sum[(eu,t)|t>element(Periods,1),Pi(eu,t)])*PrdMin / 60*0.015;
                Comment: "data unit:ton";
            }
            Variable EmissionCO2 {
                Definition: (sum[(tu,t)|t>element(Periods,1),Pi(tu,t)]+ sum[(eu,t)|t>element(Periods,1),Pi(eu,t)])*PrdMin / 60*0.997;
                Comment: "data unit:ton";
            }
            Variable EmissionSO2 {
                Definition: (sum[(tu,t)|t>element(Periods,1),Pi(tu,t)]+ sum[(eu,t)|t>element(Periods,1),Pi(eu,t)])*PrdMin / 60*0.03;
                Comment: "data unit:ton";
            }
            Variable TotalEmission {
                Definition: EmissionNOx+EmissionCO2+EmissionSO2;
            }
            Variable SunUnitFee {
                Definition: sum[(se,t),ci(se,t)];
            }
            Variable SunUnitQty {
                Definition: sum[(se,t),pi(se,t)]*PrdMin / 60;
            }
            Variable WindUnitFee {
                Definition: sum[(wd,t),ci(wd,t)];
            }
            Variable WindUnitQty {
                Definition: sum[(wd,t),pi(wd,t)]*PrdMin / 60;
            }
            Variable ThermalUnitFee {
                Definition: sum[(tu,t),ci(tu,t)];
            }
            Variable ThermalUnitQty {
                Definition: sum[(tu,t),pi(tu,t)]*PrdMin / 60;
            }
            Variable EqUnitFee {
                Definition: sum[(eu,t),ci(eu,t)];
            }
            Variable EqUnitQty {
                Definition: sum[(eu,t),pi(eu,t)]*PrdMin / 60;
            }
            Variable WaterUnitFee {
                Definition: sum[(wu,t),ci(wu,t)];
            }
            Variable WaterUnitQty {
                Definition: sum[(wu,t),pi(wu,t)]*PrdMin / 60;
            }
            Variable ThermalUnitOptCost {
                Definition: sum[(tu,t), Ci(tu,t)];
                Comment: "used to calculate the operate cost of conventional energy unit.";
            }
            Variable ThermalUnitStartCost {
                Definition: sum[(tu,t), Si(tu,t)];
                Comment: "used to calculate the start cost of conventional energy unit.";
            }
            Variable WindAndSunQty {
                Definition: (sum[(se,t),pi(se,t)]+sum[(wd,t),pi(wd,t)])*PrdMin / 60;
            }
            Variable CleanEnergyQty {
                Definition: (sum[(se,t),pi(se,t)]+sum[(wd,t),pi(wd,t)]+sum[(wu,t),pi(wu,t)])*PrdMin / 60;
            }
        }
        Set UnitSetOfWind {
            SubsetOf: EleSet;
            Index: wd;
            Definition: {
                {ele | EleType(ele) = "wd"
                        }
            }
        }
        Set UnitSetSun {
            SubsetOf: EleSet;
            Index: se;
            Definition: {
                {ele|EleType(ele) = "se"}
            }
        }

            SubsetOf: EleSet;

                {ele | EleType(ele) = "eq"
                        or EleType(ele) = "Eq"
                        or EleType(ele) = "EQ"
                        }

            Index: wu;

                {ele | EleType(ele) = "wm"
                        or EleType(ele) = "Wm"
                        or EleType(ele) = "WM" !coal or gas energy
                        }
            }
        }
        Set UnitSetWindAndSun {

                        or EleType(ele) = "se"
                        }
            }

        Set UnitSetCoalWater {

                        or EleType(ele)="wm"!water energy.
                        }
            }
        }
        Set UnitSetOfThermalUnit {
            SubsetOf: EleSet;
            Index: tu;
            Definition: {
                {ele | EleType(ele) = "un"
                        or EleType(ele) = "UN"
                        or EleType(ele) = "Un" !coal
                        or EleType(ele)="gs" !gas energy !xuebike edit 20150520
                        }
            }
        }
        Set UnitSetProvidedRsv {
            SubsetOf: EleSet;
            Index: rsvUnit;
            Definition: {
                {ele | EleType(ele) = "un"
                        or EleType(ele) = "UN"
                        or EleType(ele) = "Un" !coal
                        or EleType(ele)="gs" !gas energy  !!xuebike edit 20150414
                        or EleType(ele)="wm"!water energy.
                
                        or EleType(ele)="eq" !!eq thermal unit

                        }

        }

                        or EleType(ele) = "Un"

        Section greenPower_proc {
            Procedure e_file_out {
                Body: {
                    if(IsOpt=0)then
                    	put e_file_out_finish_cal;
                    	e_file_out_finish_cal.pagewidth:=5000;
                    	put "[cal_status]",/;
                    	put "cal_status=-1";!!Input datas  are error!
                    	putclose;
                    	return;
                    endif;
                    
                    switch FeeLeast.ProgramStatus do
                    
                            'Optimal' ,'Integersolution':
                                    put e_file_out_result;
                                    e_file_out_result.pagewidth:=5000;
                    
                                    put "<cal_period_def>" , /;
                                    put "@ Id PrdId Time" , /;
                                    index_output := 1 ;
                                    for( t | t>'past' ) do
                    			put "# ";
                    			put FormatString("%e" , index_output) , " " ;
                                            put FormatString("%i",Ord(t,Periods)-1)," ";
                    			put Period_Time(t),/;
                    			index_output:=index_output+1;
                                    endfor;!for( t | t>'past' )
                                    put "</cal_period_def>" , /;
                    
                    
                                    put "<node_lmp>" , /;
                                    put "@ Id NodeId NodeName PrdId LMP SystemEnergyPrice CongestionPrice LossPrice" , /;
                                    index_output := 1 ;
                                    for( t | t>'past' ) do
                                            for( nd ) do
                                                    put "# ";
                                                    put FormatString("%e" , index_output) , " " ;
                                                    put FormatString("%e" , nd) , " " ;
                                                    put nodename(nd), " " ;
                                                    put FormatString("%i",Ord(t,Periods)-1)," ";
                                                    put Lmp(nd,t), " " ;
                                                    put SystemEnergyPrice(t), " " ;
                                                    put CongestionPrice(nd,t), " " ;
                                                    put LossPrice(nd,t),/;
                                                    index_output:=index_output+1;
                                            endfor;!for(nd)
                                    endfor;!for( t | t>'past' )
                                    put "</node_lmp>" , /;
                    
                                    put "<unit_clearing_result>" , /;
                                    put "@ ID UnId UnName PrdId OnOff Power OperateRsvCap SyncRsvCap NonSyncCap RegulationCap LMP" , /;
                                    index_output := 1 ;
                                    for( t | t>'past' ) do
                                            for( i ) do
                                                    put "# ";
                                                    put FormatString("%e" , index_output) , " " ;
                                                    put FormatString("%e" , i) , " " ;
                                                    put cName(i), " " ;
                                                    put FormatString("%i",Ord(t,Periods)-1)," ";
                                                    put FormatString("%i" , Ui(i,t)) , " " ;
                                                    put Pi(i,t)," ";
                                                    put FormatString("%i" , 0) , " " ;
                                                    put FormatString("%i" , 0) , " " ;
                                                    put FormatString("%i" , 0) , " " ;
                                                    put FormatString("%i" , 0) , " " ;
                                                    put GenLmp(i,t),/;
                                                    index_output:=index_output+1;
                                            endfor;!for(i)
                                    endfor;!for( t | t>'past' )
                                    put "</unit_clearing_result>" , /;
                    
                    		put "<sys_mcp_result>" , /;
                                    put "@ ID PrdId SrMcp NsrMcp RMcp RMpcp RMccp OrMcp" , /;
                                    index_output := 1 ;
                                    for( t | t>'past' ) do
                                            put "# ";
                                            put FormatString("%e" , index_output) , " " ;
                                            put FormatString("%i",Ord(t,Periods)-1)," ";
                                            put FormatString("%i" , 0) , " " ;
                                            put FormatString("%i" , 0) , " " ;
                                            put FormatString("%i" , 0) , " " ;
                                            put FormatString("%i" , 0) , " " ;
                                            put FormatString("%i" , 0) , " " ;
                                            put FormatString("%i" , 0),/;
                                    	index_output:=index_output+1;
                                    endfor;!for( t | t>'past' )
                                    put "</sys_mcp_result>" , /;
                    
                                     put "<unit_credit_stat>" , /;
                                    put "@ ID UnId UnName PrdId Credit" , /;
                                    index_output := 1 ;
                                    for( t | t>'past' ) do
                                            for( i ) do
                                                    put "# ";
                                                    put FormatString("%e" , index_output) , " " ;
                                                    put FormatString("%e" , i) , " " ;
                                                    put cName(i), " " ;
                                                    put FormatString("%i",Ord(t,Periods)-1)," ";
                                                    put GenTimeSellFee(i,t),/;
                                            	index_output:=index_output+1;
                                            endfor;!for(i)
                                    endfor;!for( t | t>'past' )
                                    put "</unit_credit_stat>" , /;
                    
                                    put "<load_charge_stat>" , /;
                                    put "@ ID NodeId NodeName PrdId Power Charge" , /;
                                    index_output := 1 ;
                                    for( t | t>'past' ) do
                                            for( nd ) do
                                                    put "# ";
                                                    put FormatString("%e" , index_output) , " " ;
                                                    put FormatString("%e" , nd) , " " ;
                                                    put nodename(nd), " " ;
                                                    put FormatString("%i",Ord(t,Periods)-1)," ";
                                                    put BusLoad(nd,t), " " ;
                                                    put LoadTimeBuyFee(nd,t),/;
                                            	index_output:=index_output+1;
                                            endfor;!for(nd)
                                    endfor;!for( t | t>'past' )
                                    put "</load_charge_stat>" , /;
                    
                    
                                    put "<sys_surplus_stat>" , /;
                                    put "@ ID SysSurplus" , /;
                                    index_output := 1 ;
                                    put "# ";
                                    put FormatString("%e" , index_output) , " " ;
                                    put SysSurplus,/;
                                    put "</sys_surplus_stat>" , /;
                    
                                    putclose;
                    
                                    put e_file_out_finish_cal;
                                    e_file_out_finish_cal.pagewidth:=5000;
                                    put "[cal_status]",/;
                                    put "cal_status=0";
                                    putclose;
                    
                            'LocallyOptimal':
                                    put e_file_out_result;
                                    e_file_out_result.pagewidth:=5000;
                                    put "The results are LocallyOptima:";
                                    putclose;
                    
                                    put e_file_out_finish_cal;
                                    e_file_out_finish_cal.pagewidth:=5000;
                                    put "[cal_status]",/;
                                    put "cal_status=1";
                                    putclose;
                    
                            'Unbounded', 'Infeasible', 'IntegerInfeasible','LocallyInfeasible':
                                    put e_file_out_result;
                                    e_file_out_result.pagewidth:=5000;
                                    put "The results is Infeasible or Unbounded or IntegerInfeasible orLocallyInfeasible" ;
                                    putclose;
                    
                                    put e_file_out_finish_cal;
                                    e_file_out_finish_cal.pagewidth:=5000;
                                    put "[cal_status]",/;
                                    put "cal_status=2";
                                    putclose;
                    
                    
                            'IntermediateInfeasible', 'IntermediateNonInteger', 'IntermediateNonOptimal' :
                                    put e_file_out_result;
                                    e_file_out_result.pagewidth:=5000;
                                    put "The results is IntermediateInfeasible or IntermediateNonInteger or IntermediateNonOptimal";
                                    putclose;
                    
                                    put e_file_out_finish_cal;
                                    e_file_out_finish_cal.pagewidth:=5000;
                                    put "[cal_status]",/;
                                    put "cal_status=3";
                                    putclose;
                    
                            default :
                                    put e_file_out_result;
                                    e_file_out_result.pagewidth:=5000;
                                    put "The results are Not solved" ;
                                    putclose;
                    
                                    put e_file_out_finish_cal;
                                    e_file_out_finish_cal.pagewidth:=5000;
                                    put "[cal_status]",/;
                                    put "cal_status=4";
                                    putclose;
                    endswitch;
                }
                Comment: "xuebike edit 20150520";
            }
            Procedure e_scuc_result_out {
                Body: {
                    if(IsOpt=0)then
                    	put e_file_out_scuc_finish_cal;
                    	e_file_out_scuc_finish_cal.pagewidth:=5000;

                                                    index_output:=index_output+1;

                                    putclose;
                    
                                    /*

                "!xuebike edit 20150620"

                Definition: 10000000;
            }
            Parameter TotalCap {
                IndexDomain: t;
                Definition: {
                    !sum[i,Capacity(i)]
                }
            }
            Constraint PowerBiasCons1 {
                IndexDomain: (i,t)|t>Element(Periods,2);
                Definition: Pi(i,t)-Pi(i,t-1)=PowerBiasPlus(i,t)-PowerBiasMinus(i,t);
            }
            Constraint PowerBiasCons2 {
                IndexDomain: (i,t)|t>Element(Periods,2);
                Definition: PowerBiasMinus(i,t)+PowerBiasPlus(i,t)<=abs(Load(t)-Load(t-1))*Capacity(i)/TotalCap(t)+PowerBiasRelax(i,t);
            }
            Variable PowerBiasMinus {
                IndexDomain: (i,t);
                Range: nonnegative;
            }
            Variable PowerBiasPlus {
                IndexDomain: (i,t);
                Range: nonnegative;
            }
            Variable PowerBiasRelax {
                IndexDomain: (i,t);
                Range: nonnegative;
            }
            Set PowerBiasConsSet {
                SubsetOf: AllConstraints;
                Definition: {
                    data
                    {PowerBiasCons1,PowerBiasCons2
                    }
                }
            }

            Section TUnitPriceInput {

                            !xuebike edit 20150807
                        }
                    }

                        IndexDomain: (i,l);
                    }

                        }

                ExternalProcedure get_unitprice_data_ext {
                    Arguments: (a);
                    DllName: DllFileName;
                    BodyCall: Get_UnitPrice_Data(scalar : a );
                    Parameter a {
                        Range: {
                            {1..inf}
                        }
                        Property: Input;
                    }
                }
                ExternalFunction get_unitprice_num_ext {
                    Arguments: (path);
                    DllName: DllFileName;
                    ReturnType: integer;
                    BodyCall: Get_UnitPrice_Num(scalar : path);
                    StringParameter path {
                        Property: Input;
                    }
                }
                Procedure UnitPrice_Init {
                    Body: {
                        UnitPriceNum := get_unitprice_num_ext(Path_in);
                        
                        index_temp := 1;
                        while(index_temp <= UnitPriceNum) do
                                get_unitprice_data_ext(index_temp);
                        
                                UnitSet_ele := StringToElement (ThermalUnitSet , UnitName_Input , create : 0);
                                PriceBlockSet_ele := Element (CostBlockSet , PriceId_Input);
                                Periods_ele := Element (Periods , PrdId_Input + 1);
                        
                                if (IsMultiCost = 1) then
                                        UnitIncPrice( UnitSet_ele , PriceBlockSet_ele , Periods_ele) := UnitPrice_inccost_Input;
                                        PriceBlockStart( UnitSet_ele , PriceBlockSet_ele , Periods_ele) := UnitPrice_out1_Input;
                                        PriceBlockEnd( UnitSet_ele , PriceBlockSet_ele , Periods_ele) := UnitPrice_out2_Input;
                                        UnitBasePrice( UnitSet_ele , PriceBlockSet_ele , Periods_ele):=UnitPrice_netcost_Input; !xuebike edit 20150807
                        
                                else
                                        Reg_UnitIncPrice( UnitSet_ele , PriceBlockSet_ele ) := UnitPrice_inccost_Input;
                                        Reg_PriceBlockStart( UnitSet_ele , PriceBlockSet_ele ) := UnitPrice_out1_Input;
                                        Reg_PriceBlockEnd( UnitSet_ele , PriceBlockSet_ele ) := UnitPrice_out2_Input;
                        		Reg_UnitNetFee( UnitSet_ele , PriceBlockSet_ele ) :=UnitPrice_netcost_Input;!xuebike edit 20150807
                        
                                        UnitIncPrice( UnitSet_ele , PriceBlockSet_ele , t) := Reg_UnitIncPrice( UnitSet_ele , PriceBlockSet_ele );
                                        PriceBlockStart( UnitSet_ele , PriceBlockSet_ele , t) := Reg_PriceBlockStart( UnitSet_ele , PriceBlockSet_ele );
                                        PriceBlockEnd( UnitSet_ele , PriceBlockSet_ele , t) := Reg_PriceBlockEnd( UnitSet_ele , PriceBlockSet_ele );
                        		UnitBasePrice( UnitSet_ele , PriceBlockSet_ele , t):= Reg_UnitNetFee( UnitSet_ele , PriceBlockSet_ele ); !xuebike edit 20150807
                                endif;
                                index_temp += 1;
                        endwhile;
                    }
                }
            }

            Procedure CalTotalCap {
                Body: {
                    for t  do
                      for i do
                        if(((i,t) in FixedOnOffSet) and FixedOnOffList(i,t)=0 )then
                             TotalCap(t):=TotalCap(t)+0;
                        elseif((i,t) in FixedScheduleSet) then
                             TotalCap(t):=TotalCap(t)+FixedOutPutPower(i,t);
                        else
                        	 TotalCap(t):=TotalCap(t)+Capacity(i);
                        endif;
                    
                      endfor;
                    endfor;
                }
                Comment: "xuebike edit 20150620";
            }
        }

    DeclarationSection LMPDeclaration {
        Set LMPSolutionConsSet {
            SubsetOf: AllConstraints;
        }
        Set LMPDependentVariSet {
            SubsetOf: AllVariables;
            Definition: {
                data
                {
                   !!begin dependent variables.
                   Fee
                
                   !!end of dependent varivables.
                }
            }
        }
        Parameter ScoreOfBid {
            IndexDomain: (i);
            Range: free;
            Definition: (sum[(nd,t),NodeGenList(nd,i)*lmp(nd,t)*pi(i,t)]-  (sum[(l,t), UnitIncCost(i,l,t)*pli(i,l,t)] ))/(sum[(t),pi(i,t)]+0.000001);
        }
        Set LMPSolutionVariSet {
            SubsetOf: AllVariables;
            Definition: {
                
                data
                {
                   !!begin independent variables.
                   pli,
                
                   !!end of independent varivables.
                
                
                   !!begin dependent variables
                    Pi,Fee,NdPowerOfGen,Ci,Si
                
                   !!end of dependent variables.
                
                }
            }
        }
        Set NetworkNodeSet {
            Index: nd;
            OrderBy: nd;
        }
        Set LinesSet {
            Index: ln;
            OrderBy: ln;
        }
        Parameter GenAdjustedBidPrice {
            IndexDomain: (i,l,t);
            Definition: sum[nd|NodeGenList(nd,i),SysLossSens(nd,t)]*UnitIncCost(i,l,t);
        }
        Parameter NodeGenList {
            IndexDomain: (nd,i);
            Range: binary;
        }
        Variable NdPowerOfGen {
            IndexDomain: (nd,t);
        }
        Parameter BusLoad {
            IndexDomain: (nd,t);
            Range: nonnegative;
        }
        Parameter LinePowerUpLimit {
            IndexDomain: (ln);
        }
        Parameter LinePowerDownLimit {
            IndexDomain: (ln);
        }
        Parameter PTDFSens {
            IndexDomain: (nd,ln,t);
        }
        Parameter SysLossSens {
            IndexDomain: (nd,t);
        }
        Parameter SysTotalLoss {
            IndexDomain: (t);
        }
        Variable Fee {
            Definition: {
                !(sum[(i,l,t), UnitIncCost(i,l,t)*pli(i,l,t)] )
                
                
                sum[(i,t), Ci(i,t)+Si(i,t)]
            }
        }
        MathematicalProgram FeeLeast {
            Objective: Fee;
            Direction: minimize;
            Constraints: LMPSolutionConsSet;
            Variables: LMPSolutionVariSet;
            Type: LP;
        }
        MathematicalProgram UCFeeLeast {
            Objective: Fee;
            Direction: minimize;
            Constraints: LMPSolutionConsSet;
            Type: MIP;
        }
        Constraint piConstraint {
            IndexDomain: (i,t);
            Definition: {
                !pi(i,t)=CostBlockStart(i,first(CostBlockSet),t)+ sum [l, pli(i,l,t)]
                pi(i,t)=Ui(i,t)*CostBlockStart(i,first(CostBlockSet),t)+ sum [l, pli(i,l,t)]
            }
        }
        Constraint GenMaxPowerCons {
            IndexDomain: (i,t);
            Definition: Pi(i,t)<=Pmax(i,t)*Ui(i,t);
        }
        Constraint GenMinPowerCons {
            IndexDomain: (i,t);
            Definition: Pi(i,t)>=Pmin(i,t)*Ui(i,t);
        }
        Constraint PowerBalanceCons {
            IndexDomain: t;
            Property: ShadowPrice;
            Definition: sum [i,Pi(i,t)]=sum [nd,BusLoad(nd,t)]+SysTotalLoss(t);
        }
        Constraint NdPowerCons {
            IndexDomain: (nd,t);
            Definition: NdPowerOfGen(nd,t)=sum[i|NodeGenList(nd,i),Pi(i,t)];
        }
        Constraint LinePowerUpCons {
            IndexDomain: (ln,t);
            Property: ShadowPrice;
            Definition: sum[nd,PTDFSens(nd,ln,t)*[NdPowerOfGen(nd,t)-BusLoad(nd,t)]]<=LinePowerUpLimit(ln);
        }
        Constraint LinePowerDownCons {
            IndexDomain: (ln,t);
            Definition: LinePowerDownLimit(ln)<=sum[nd,PTDFSens(nd,ln,t)*[NdPowerOfGen(nd,t)-BusLoad(nd,t)]];
        }
    }
    DeclarationSection IODeclaration {
        StringParameter ErrorStr;
        Parameter ExcelStatus;
        StringParameter NodeName {
            IndexDomain: nd;
        }
        StringParameter GenName {
            IndexDomain: (i);
        }
        StringParameter LineName {
            IndexDomain: (ln);
        }
        StringParameter LineNodeF {

            IndexDomain: (ln);

    DeclarationSection LMPCompenents {
        Parameter SystemEnergyPrice {
            IndexDomain: (t);
            Definition: PowerBalanceCons(t).ShadowPrice;
        }
        Parameter LossPrice {
            IndexDomain: (nd,t);
            Definition: SystemEnergyPrice(t)*(1/SysLossSens(nd,t)-1);
        }
        Parameter CongestionPrice {
            IndexDomain: (nd,t);
            Definition: {
                sum[ln,PTDFSens(nd,ln,t)*
                  (LinePowerUpCons(ln,t).ShadowPrice
                           !-LinePowerDownCons(ln).ShadowPrice
                      )]
            }
        }
        Parameter Lmp {
            IndexDomain: (nd,t);
            Definition: SystemEnergyPrice(t)+CongestionPrice(nd,t)+LossPrice(nd,t);
        }
    }
    DeclarationSection LMPStatDeclaration {
        Parameter GenLmp {
            IndexDomain: (i,t);
            Definition: sum[nd|NodeGenList(nd,i),Lmp(nd,t)];
        }
        Parameter LoadTimeBuyFee {
            IndexDomain: (nd,t);
            Definition: BusLoad(nd,t)*Lmp(nd,t);
        }
        Parameter GenTimeSellFee {
            IndexDomain: (i,t);
            Definition: pi(i,t)*sum[nd|NodeGenList(nd,i),Lmp(nd,t)];
        }
        Parameter LoadBuyFee {
            IndexDomain: (nd);
            Definition: sum[t,BusLoad(nd,t)*Lmp(nd,t)];
        }
        Parameter GenSellFee {
            IndexDomain: (i);
            Definition: sum[t,pi(i,t)*sum[nd|NodeGenList(nd,i),Lmp(nd,t)]];
        }
        Parameter SysSurplus {
            Definition: sum[(nd,t),LoadTimeBuyFee(nd,t)]-sum[(i,t),GenTimeSellFee(i,t)];
        }
    }

            Body: {
                 LMPSolutionConsSet+=
                data
                {
                  PowerBalanceCons,NdPowerCons,!TieLineFixedPowerCons,lmp
                  LinePowerUpCons
                }
                +LMPDependentVariSet
                + UCConstraintsSet;
            }
        }

            Body: {
                WorkbookName:=FormatString("%s\\DataIn.xls",Path_in);

                ExcelRetrieveSet(WorkbookName,NetworkNodeSet,"Node_NodeIdRng");
                ExcelRetrieveTable(WorkbookName,NodeName,"Node_NodeNameRng","Node_NodeIdRng");
                
                /*

                ExcelRetrieveSet(WorkbookName,GenSet,"Gen_GenidRng");
                ExcelRetrieveTable(WorkbookName,GenName,"Gen_GenNameRng","Gen_GenidRng");

                ExcelRetrieveTable(WorkbookName,Pmin,"Gen_PminRng","Gen_GenidRng");
                */
                
                ExcelSetActiveSheet(WorkbookName,"NdGenList");
                ExcelRetrieveTable(WorkbookName,NodeGenList,"NdGenList_IsGenLinkToNodeRng","NdGenList_NodeGenIdRng");
                
                 ExcelSetActiveSheet(WorkbookName,"Load");
                ExcelRetrieveTable(WorkbookName,BusLoad,"Load_LoadDefRng","Load_NodeIdPrdRng");
                
                ExcelSetActiveSheet(WorkbookName,"Line");

                ExcelRetrieveTable(WorkbookName,LineName,"Line_LineNameRng","Line_LineIdRng");
                ExcelRetrieveTable(WorkbookName,LineNodeF,"Line_NodeFRng","Line_LineIdRng");
                ExcelRetrieveTable(WorkbookName,LineNodeT,"Line_NodeTRng","Line_LineIdRng");
                ExcelRetrieveTable(WorkbookName,LinePowerUpLimit,"Line_UpLimitRng","Line_LineIdRng");
                
                 ExcelSetActiveSheet(WorkbookName,"PTDFSens");
                ExcelRetrieveTable(WorkbookName,PTDFSens,"PTDFSens_SensRng","PTDFSens_NodeLineIdPrdRng");
                
                ExcelSetActiveSheet(WorkbookName,"SysLossPenaltyFactor");
                ExcelRetrieveTable(WorkbookName,SysLossSens,"SysLossPenaltyFactor_LossPF","SysLossPenaltyFactor_NodeIdPrdRng");
                
                ExcelSetActiveSheet(WorkbookName,"SysTotalLoss");
                ExcelRetrieveTable(WorkbookName,SysTotalLoss,"SysTotalLossRng","SysTotalLoss_PrdRng");
                
                /*

                ExcelRetrieveTable(WorkbookName,GenBidBlockEnd,"GenBid_GenBidEndRng","GenBid_GenIdBidSegIdPrdRng");
                ExcelRetrieveTable(WorkbookName,GenBidBlockPrice,"GenBid_GenBidPriceRng","GenBid_GenIdBidSegIdPrdRng");
                */
                
                ExcelCloseWorkbook(WorkbookName,0);
            }
        }

            Body: {
                for t|t>element(Periods,2) do

                  SysLossSens(nd,t):=SysLossSens(nd,element(Periods,2));
                endfor;
            }

            Procedure BusLoad_Init {
                Body: {
                     BusLoadNum:= get_busload_num_ext(Path_in);
                    
                    index_temp := 1;
                    while(index_temp <= BusLoadNum) do
                            get_busload_data_ext(index_temp);
                    
                            NodeId_ele := StringToElement(NetworkNodeSet, NodeId_Input , create :1) ;
                    
                            Periods_ele := Element (Periods , Prd_Input + 1);
                            BusLoad(NodeId_ele, Periods_ele ):=LoadDef_Input;
                    
                            index_temp += 1;
                    endwhile;
                }
            }
            ExternalFunction get_busload_num_ext {
                Arguments: (path);
                DllName: DllFileName;
                ReturnType: integer;
                BodyCall: Get_BusLoad_Num(scalar : path);
                StringParameter path {
                    Property: Input;
                }
            }
            ExternalProcedure get_busload_data_ext {

                        {1..inf}

        }
        Section LineInput {
            DeclarationSection LineParam {
                Parameter LineNum {
                    Range: integer;
                }
                StringParameter LineId_Input;
                StringParameter LineName_Input;
                StringParameter NODE_F_Input;
                StringParameter NODE_T_Input;
                Parameter UpLimit_Input;
                ElementParameter LineId_ele {
                    Range: LinesSet;
                }
            }
            Procedure Line_Init {
                Body: {
                    LineNum:= get_line_num_ext(Path_in);
                    
                    index_temp := 1;
                    while(index_temp <=LineNum) do
                            get_line_data_ext(index_temp);
                            LineId_ele := StringToElement(LinesSet, LineId_Input , create :1) ;
                    	LineName(LineId_ele):=LineName_Input;
                    	LineNodeF(LineId_ele):=NODE_F_Input;
                    	LineNodeT(LineId_ele):=NODE_T_Input;
                    	LinePowerUpLimit(LineId_ele):=UpLimit_Input;
                            index_temp += 1;
                    endwhile;
                }
            }
            ExternalFunction get_line_num_ext {
                Arguments: (path);
                DllName: DllFileName;
                ReturnType: integer;
